   <font color=red><strong>attach importance to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：attach importance to“重视”。"attach importance to"是一个常用的短语，表示赋予某事物重要性或重视某事物。通常用于表达对某事的看法或态度，强调其重要性或优先级。</strong></font>

   **例如：**

   - **It's important to attach importance to your health and wellbeing. （关注健康和福祉很重要。）**
   - **Our company attaches great importance to customer satisfaction. （我们公司非常重视客户满意度。）**
   - **We should attach more importance to environmental protection. （我们应该更加重视环境保护。）**

3. She <u><font color=red><strong>        has been considering          </strong></font></u> how to get that precious chance all the morning,  but she hasn't come up with any idea yet.  (consider)

   整个上午，她**一直在考虑**如何得到那个宝贵的机会，但是她还是没有想出任何办法。

   <font color=red><strong>has been considering</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示从过去某个时间开始一直持续到现在的动作应用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

   <strong>"Come up with" 是一个常用的短语，表示“想出（某个主意、想法或解决方案）”。常常用于描述某人在需要解决问题或寻找创新想法时所做的努力。The team spent weeks trying to come up with a new advertising campaign. （团队花费了数周时间尝试想出一项新的广告宣传方案。）</strong>

4. Oh,it's you, Ella! Your voice <u><font color=red><strong>      sounds different       </strong></font></u> from on the phone. What's happening? (different)

   哦,是你,埃拉!你的声音从电话里**听起来不同**。发生什么事了?

   <font color=red><strong>sounds different</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：sound此处为系动词,后用形容词 different作表语。</strong></font>

5. Seeing the sun <u><font color=red><strong>       rising from behind        </strong></font></u> the mountain, we let out a cry of joy. （rise)

   看着太阳**从**那座山**后升起**, 我们高兴地欢呼起来。

   <font color=red><strong>rising from behind</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：see后可跟动词ing形式作宾语补足语,表示动作正在进行。这句话的句首的非谓语动词是 "Seeing"，作为一个现在分词，用作状语，表示时间状语，描述主句中的情境。</strong></font>

6. Choosing what to eat is no longer as hard as before，but I still <u><font color=red><strong>      advise you to have      </strong></font></u> more healthy food. (advise)

   选择吃什么再也不像以前那么难了,但是我仍然**建议你**多**吃**健康的食物

   <font color=red><strong>advise you to have/eat; advise (that you (should)have/eat</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：advise后可跟不定式作宾语补足语,也可后跟宾语从句,从句应用虚拟语气,即谓语动词用“should+动词原形”，should可省略</strong></font>

7. When it comes to Internet language, language experts hold the view <u><font color=red><strong>        that it has a great influence on            </strong></font></u> the development of language. (influence)

   说到网络语言,语言专家认为**它对**语言的发展**有很大的影响**。

   <font color=red><strong>that it has a great influence on/that it greatly influences</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：that引导同位语从句,用来解释说明 view的内容, that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略; have a great influence on“对……有巨大影响”,相当于greatly influence.例如：Technology has a great influence on our daily lives. (科技对我们的日常生活有很大的影响。)</strong></font>

   <strong>"When it comes to"是一个常用的短语，通常用于引出某个话题或问题，表示进入某个话题或问题时的过渡。它的意思是"涉及到、提到、谈到"。这个短语通常用于口语和书面语中，特别是在演讲、文章或讨论中，可以用来引出一个话题或问题，以吸引听众或读者的注意力。When it comes to learning a foreign language, practice is the key to success.</strong>

8. <u><font color=red><strong>         Seated in the sofa        </strong></font></u> was the so-called gentleman with his hands playing with some cards.  (seat)

   **坐在沙发上的**手中玩着纸牌的是那个所谓的绅士。

   <font color=red><strong>Seated in the sofa</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：分析句子成分可知,句中用了倒装语序,此处seated为形容词化的动词-ed形式,说明主语的状态。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>这句话的主语是 "the so-called gentleman"，谓语是 "was"，表示他处于被动状态并且在沙发上坐着。"Seated in the sofa" 是一个过去分词短语，用来描述这位绅士的位置。接下来是一个定语从句 "with his hands playing with some cards"，修饰 "the so-called gentleman"，说明他正在玩纸牌。</strong></font>

   <strong>在这个句子中，"seated"是过去分词短语，用来修饰主语"the so-called gentleman"，表明他是坐在沙发上的，是一个被动的状态。相比之下，如果用"-ing"形式作为形容词修饰主语，则表达的是主语正在进行的动作。例如，"The gentleman was sitting in the sofa, playing with some cards." 这句话表达的是主语正在坐在沙发上，并同时玩着牌。因此，使用过去分词和"-ing"形式修饰主语的区别在于强调状态和行为的不同。</strong>

9. It is still unknown  <u><font color=red><strong>        if she can set aside         </strong></font></u> some time to visit her sick father. (set）

   还不知道**她是否能省出**一些时间去看望她生病的父亲。

   <font color=red><strong>whether/if she can set aside</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：it在句中作形式主语，真正的主语是后面的从句,whether/if引导主语从句,意为“是否”;</strong></font>

   <strong>set aside“省出,留出”。</strong>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>          Under the command of             </strong></font></u> Zheng He,  the fleets set sail from the South China Sea across the Indian Ocean to the mouth of the Red Sea,  and traveled further South,  discovering the eastern coast of Africa.  (under)

    **在**郑和**的指挥下**,  船队从中国南海起航,  横穿印度洋，到达红海人海口,并继续向南航行,发现了非洲东海岸。

    <font color=red><strong>Under the command of</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：under the command of“在…·…的指挥下”。</strong></font>

## lesson 21

1. That night I spent most of my time <u><font color=red><strong>   in sitting there      </strong></font></u> ,  doing my homework.（sit)

   那天晚上,我花了大部分时间**坐在那里**做作业。

   <font color=red><strong>(in) sitting there</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：spend some time in doing sth.“花费多少时间做某事”,其中in可省略。</strong></font>

2. Only by discovering what we do best  <u><font color=red><strong>    can we hope to        </strong></font></u> reach our goals and truly make a difference. (hope)

   只有通过发现我们所擅长做的事情,我们**才能有希望**实现我们的目标,真正有所作为。

   <font color=red><strong>can we hope to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：only强调状语置于句首时句子用部分倒装;hope后跟不定式作宾语。</strong></font>

   <strong>"Make a difference" 是一个常见的英语短语，意思是“产生影响”、“有所不同”，通常用于强调某个行动、决策或想法可以对某个情况、问题或结果产生重要影响。它也可以表示一个人或一件事情与众不同，具有独特的影响力或价值。Your hard work can really make a difference in the success of this project.(你的辛勤工作真的会对这个项目的成功产生影响。)</strong>

3. From then on I went all out to spend every minute available practicing my oral English <u><font color=red><strong>       as my teacher suggested      </strong></font></u> (suggest)

   从那时起,我就竭尽全力利用可能的每一分钟**按照我老师建议**的练习口语。

   <font color=red><strong>as my teacher suggested/the way my teacher suggested</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：本句是一个方式状语从句,as表示“正如”;也可用the way my teacher suggested。</strong></font>

   <strong>"go all out" 是一个固定短语，表示“全力以赴，竭尽全力”，意思是尽最大的努力去做某件事情。在这个句子中，“went all out” 的意思是这个人尽可能利用所有可用的时间去练习口语英语，表示这个人非常用心和努力。</strong>

   <strong>"As"引导方式状语从句，表示某个行为或情况的方式或方式，通常与主句中的动词相呼应。这种从句中的谓语动词常用动词的-ing 形式。例如，"She sang as if she were on stage."（她唱歌的方式好像是在舞台上一样）"As"引导的状语从句也可以表示时间、原因、条件等。</strong>

4. He has been doing his homework for a long time. I think he <u><font color=red><strong>     must be tired         </strong></font></u> now. (tired)

   这么长时间他一直都在做作业。我想现在他**一定累了**。

   <font color=red><strong>must be tired</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示对现在情况的肯定推测用must do。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"must have done"是一个情态动词的形式，用于表示对过去发生的事情的推测和猜测。这种结构常常用于推测某个过去事件，但没有确凿的证据。例如：He must have left early this morning.（他今天早上一定离开了。）注意，"must have done"结构中的动词要使用完成时态，即"have done"，而"must"本身是情态动词，不具有时态，只有一个形式。</strong></font>

5. Joe <u><font color=red><strong>    was reading a book         </strong></font></u> when he suddenly heard someone breaking the window. (read)

   乔**正在读一本书**, 突然听见有人砸窗户。

   <font color=red><strong>was reading a book</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示过去某个时间正在进行的动作应用过去进行时。</strong></font>

6. The train ran over and killed a boy and his dog <u><font color=red><strong>       that were crossing    </strong></font></u> the track.(cross)

   火车轧死了**正在穿过**铁轨的男孩和他的狗。

   <font color=red><strong>that were crossing</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：先行词既有人又有物,故只能用that引导定语从句, that在从句中作主语,不能省略;也可直接用动词-ing形式作后置定语。</strong></font>

7. The girl was upset at the final result，with her eyes <u><font color=red><strong>          filled with tears            </strong></font></u> ．(fill)

   这个女孩对于最终结果很难过,眼睛里**充满了泪水**。

   <font color=red><strong>filled with tears</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：题干中的with暗示用“with十宾语十宾语补足语”这一独立主格结构,且fill与eyes之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用动词-ed形式作宾语补足语;</strong></font>

   <strong>fill...with..“用……把·……装满/填满”。</strong>

8. He said that the driver must have had an accident; otherwise he <u><font color=red><strong>       would have arrived         </strong></font></u>by then. （arrive)

   他说这个司机一定出了事故,否则他那时**就已经到达了**。

   <font color=red><strong>would/could/should/might have arrived</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：由语境可知,此处是对过去情况的虚拟,此时主句应用could/would/should/might have done的形式。</strong></font>

9. It's a long way to go，and there is nobody else together with you.  <u><font color=red><strong>        what if      </strong></font></u> the car breaks down? (if)

   这是一段很长的路,而且没有人和你一起。**如果**车坏了怎么办?

   <font color=red><strong>What if</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：What if...?“要是……怎么办?”</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>      What we all know           </strong></font></u> is that the old scientist, for whom life was difficult in the past，still works very hard in his eighties. (know)

    **我们都知道**，那个过去生活很艰苦的老科学家，在80多岁的时候仍然非常努力地工作

    <font color=red><strong>What is known to us all/What we all know</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：what引导主语从句,并在从句中作主语/宾语。</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>eighties：表示八十几岁</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>介词短语 "for whom" 可以用作定语从句的引导词，用来修饰先行词，说明先行词所属或者具有的特征。一般来说，先行词为人，介词短语 "for whom" 后面跟着一个代词或名词，表示先行词是这个代词或名词的对象或者拥有者。</strong></font>
    
    例如：
    
    - **The school is looking for a volunteer, for whom the ability to speak multiple languages is highly desirable.（学校正在寻找一名志愿者，他能够说多种语言是非常希望的。）**
    - **The scholarship is awarded to students who come from low-income families, for whom financial assistance is essential.（奖学金授予那些来自低收入家庭，需要财政援助的学生。）**
    - **The company provides free training courses for employees, for whom career development is a top priority.（公司为员工提供免费的培训课程，他们的职业发展是最重要的事情之一。）**
    
    <font color=red><strong>在这些例子中，介词短语 "for whom" 后面跟着的代词或名词（ability, financial assistance, career development）表明了先行词（volunteer, students, employees）的某种特征或拥有情况。</strong></font>

# part 04

## lesson 22

1. The time has come at last <u><font color=red><strong>          when we can make good use of            </strong></font></u> nuclear energy. (make)

   **我们可以好好利用**核能的时代终于来了。

   <font color=red><strong>when we can make good use of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：make good use of“好好利用”;定语从句的先行词是表示时间的the time,引导词在从句中作时间状语,故用 when.</strong></font>

2. It was not until I was in his place  <u><font color=red><strong>      that I understood          </strong></font></u> what it really meant to him.（understand)

   直到我处在他的位置我**才明白**这对于他来说真正意味着什么。

   <font color=red><strong>that I understood</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：此处是It was not until... that...强调句,句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>

   **如果"Not until"句型和强调句式结合使用，通常that后面的部分不需要倒装。例如：It was not until yesterday that I realized how much I love him.（强调句中，动词"realized"并没有被倒装）**

   **如果"Not until"句型后面跟的是完整的陈述句，而不是强调句，那么就需要进行部分倒装，把主语和助动词调换位置。**

   - **Not until I got home did I realize that I had left my phone at the office.（注意，这里的"did"是助动词，用于构成部分倒装）**
   - **Not until she had finished her homework could she watch TV.（同样地，这里的"had"也是助动词，用于构成部分倒装）**

3. Why did so many people stand by while the woman  <u><font color=red><strong>      was being robbed          </strong></font></u>in broad daylight? (rob)

   当那位妇女在光天化日之下**遭到抢劫**时为什么那么多人只是袖手旁观?

   <font color=red><strong>was being robbed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：while“当……时”,根据题意用过去进行时。</strong></font>

4. The committee members agreed to the suggestion that the plan <u><font color=red><strong>     (should) be put into practice       </strong></font></u>at once. (practice)

   委员会成员们同意了这个计划马上**实施**的建议。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) be put into practice</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示“建议”的suggestion后的同位语从句中要用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should+动词原形”, should可以省略，参考语法3.3.1。</strong></font>

5. I'd be only too happy to help you, if I<u><font color=red><strong>          had the money             </strong></font></u>  . (have)

   如果我**有钱**的话我会非常高兴帮助你。

   <font color=red><strong>had the money</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：if条件句表示与现在事实相反的假设,谓语动词用过去式;与将来事实相反才可以用should和were to。</strong></font>

6. Seldom  <u><font color=red><strong>      did it break down             </strong></font></u> when I drove the car to the lonely village to help the left-behind children. (break)

   当我开着车去偏僻的地方帮助那些留守儿童时,**它**很少**出毛病**。

   <font color=red><strong>did it break down</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：break down“出毛病”;表示否定意义的seldom置于句首时句子用部分倒装,句中为一般过去时态。</strong></font>

7. l bet that he will come late again. <u><font color=red><strong>       It's typical of him      </strong></font></u> to do so. (typical)

   我敢说他又要迟到了。他**一贯**如此。

   <font color=red><strong>It's typical of him</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：it is typical of sb to do sth.“不出所料，特有的”。</strong></font>

8. To be honest,it is the first time that I <u><font color=red><strong>         have handed in my homework             </strong></font></u> on time. (hand)

   说实话,这是我第一次按时**交我的作业**。

   <font color=red><strong>have handed in my homework</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：在“It is the first/second time that...”句型中 that从句用现在完成时; 在句型“It/That/This was the second/third.. . time that...”中that后的从句用过去完成时; hand in“上交”。</strong></font>

9. The little girl,  who has been spoiled has got used to <u><font color=red><strong>   being offered        </strong></font></u> everything she wants. (offer)

   那个被宠坏的小女孩已经习惯了想要什么**有什么**。

   <font color=red><strong>being offered</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：get used to doing sth.“习惯做某事”;the little girl 与 offer之间是被动关系,故用动词-ing形式的被动语态。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>     Every time you smile at        </strong></font></u> someone, you give a gift to that person. （every)

    **每一次你向**某人**微笑时**,你就给了那个人一件礼物。

    <font color=red><strong>Every time you smile at</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：此处为every time引导的时间状语从句,表示“每次……的时候”</strong></font>

## lesson 23

1. Now many a student <u><font color=red><strong>      has no difficulty in        </strong></font></u> pronouncing this word. (difficulty)

   现在许多学生在这个词的发音上**没有困难**。

   <font color=red><strong>has no difficulty (in)</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析："many a+可数名词单数”作主语时,谓语动词用单数形式;</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>have no difficulty in doing sth.“做某事没有困难”,其中in可省略。</strong></font>

2. It is said that  <u><font color=red><strong>     it will take us        </strong></font></u> half a year to complete the whole trip,  so we must make full preparations for it. (take)

   据说完成整个旅行**将会花掉我们**半年的时间,因此我们必须为此做好充分的准备。

   <font color=red><strong>it will take us</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：it在 that从句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的不定式短语。It takes/took sb some time to do sth.意为“某人做某事花了多长时间”,由句意可知用一般将来时。</strong></font>

3. All the evidence pointed to the fact  <u><font color=red><strong>      that he was involved in        </strong></font></u> the crime. (involve)

   所有的证据都表明一个事实,**那就是他**与这起犯罪活动**有牵连**。

   <font color=red><strong>that he was involved in</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：that 引导同位语从句,用来解释说明fact的内容,that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略; be involved in“与……有关联”.</strong></font>

4. <u><font color=red><strong>        That he couldn't come back          </strong></font></u> on New Year's Eve disappointed all his family members. (come)

   除夕**他回不来**,这让所有的家庭成员都很失望。

   <font color=red><strong>That he couldn't come back</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：that引导主语从句,在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,且不能省略；disappoint v  使失望;使破灭;使落空</strong></font>

5. I <u><font color=red><strong>        could have bought          </strong></font></u> the new type of DVD that day,  but I didn't have enough money with me. (buy)

   那天我**本可以买下**那台新款DVD,但是我没带够钱。

   <font color=red><strong>could have bought</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：由语境可知,此处是对过去情况的虚拟,应用could have done的形式;</strong></font>

6. His words remind me  <u><font color=red><strong>        of what we did          </strong></font></u>  together during the past holidays. (what)

   他的话让我想起了在过去的假期**我们**一起**做的事情**。

   <font color=red><strong>of what we did</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：remind sb of sth.“提醒某人某事,使某人想起某事”;what引导宾语从句,作介词of的宾语,并在从句中作宾语；remain v.
   留下，逗留，停留;保持不变; n.
   （历史）遗迹，残迹;</strong></font>

7. It's no use  <u><font color=red><strong>      arguing with him       </strong></font></u> ----he never cares about what others say. (argue)

   **和他争论**是没有用的,他从来都不在乎别人说什么。

   <font color=red><strong>arguing with him</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：It's no use doing sth.“做某事是没用/徒劳的”;argue with sb.“和某人争论”。</strong></font>

8. I saw Mary twice last month,but I <u><font color=red><strong>         haven't seen          </strong></font></u> her husband recently. (see)

   上个月我看见玛丽两次,但是我最近**没见过**她丈天。

   <font color=red><strong>haven't seen</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：结合时间状语recently可知,此处表示过去已经开始,持续到现在,并且有可能继续下去的动作,应用现在完成时。</strong></font>

9. When I returned home from school yesterday, mother  <u><font color=red><strong>    happened to be cooking       </strong></font></u>  in the kitchen. (happen)

   当我昨天从学校回到家时,妈妈**碰巧**在厨房**做饭**。

   <font color=red><strong>happened to be cooking</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：happen后跟不定式作宾语;结合语境可知,此处表示正在进行的动作,故用happen to be doing的形式。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"happen to do sth" 表示“碰巧做某事”，强调行动的偶然性和意外性。例如：I happened to meet my old friend in the street yesterday.（我昨天碰巧在街上遇见了我的老朋友。）</strong></font>

10. It was the good training <u><font color=red><strong>        that she had           </strong></font></u> at school，not her great talent,  that made her a good pianist.(have)

    **是她在学校接受的**好的培训而不是她的巨大天赋,使她成了一名优秀的钢琴家。

    <font color=red><strong>(that/which) she had</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：that/which引导定语从句,并在从句中作宾语,可省略。</strong></font>





## lesson 24

1. Had it not been for the doctor's careful treatment, he <u><font color=red><strong>       wouldn't have lived      </strong></font></u> till last year. (live)

   要不是医生的精心治疗,他**不可能活到**去年。

   <font color=red><strong>couldn't/wouldn't have lived</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：由语境可知,此处是对过去情况的虚拟,应用could/would have done的形式,此处应用否定形式。</strong></font>

2. Helen <u><font color=red><strong>     struggled to her feet      </strong></font></u> after the struggle with two robbers. (struggle)

   海伦在与两个盗贼搏斗之后**挣扎着站了起来**。

   <font color=red><strong>struggled to her feet</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：struggle to one's feet“挣扎着站起来”,由句意可知用一般过去时。</strong></font>

3. Martin, who was sitting on my left,  said that this meal was the best <u><font color=red><strong>           (that) he had ever had             </strong></font></u> . (have)

   坐在我左边的马丁说这顿饭是**他曾吃过的**最好的。

   <font color=red><strong>(that) he had ever had</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：先行词为最高级时,只能用 that引导定语从句,此处that在从句中作宾语,可省略;表示在过去某一时刻或动作之前已完成的动作应用过去完成时。</strong></font>

4. The development of modern science will soon  <u><font color=red><strong>         make it possible         </strong></font></u> for some patients to recover from these illnesses. (make)

   现代科学的发展不久**就会让**一些患这些疾病的病人恢复健康**成为可能**。

   <font color=red><strong>make it possible</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：分析句子结构可知,该句真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语,故用it作形式宾语.</strong></font>

5. Other nutrients, such as fiber and minerals, help to keep  <u><font color=red><strong>     the body functioning          </strong></font></u> well. (function)

   其他营养物,如纤维和矿物质,有助于保持**身体机能**良好**运转**。

   <font color=red><strong>the body functioning </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：keep后跟动词-ing 形式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

   **通常我们使用keep sth + 形容词/副词的形式来表达“持续保持某种状态”的意思**

   1. **Keep the window closed.（保持窗户关闭。）**
   2. **She keeps her house clean.（她保持她的房子干净。）**
   3. **I try to keep fit by exercising regularly.（我试着通过定期锻炼来保持健康。）**

   **而keep sth doing这个词组则表示“保持某事物持续进行”，例如：**

   1. **They kept me waiting for hours.（他们让我等了几个小时。）**
   2. **She kept the conversation going by asking questions.（她通过问问题让对话持续进行。）**
   3. **The company keeps producing high-quality products.（该公司继续生产高品质的产品。）**

   **function：**

      **n.作用;功能;职能;机能;社交聚会;典礼;宴会;函数;子例行程序**
      **v.起作用;正常工作;运转**

6. Our English teacher is very strict with us and also is very friendly，so he  <u><font color=red><strong>        is  highly thought of         </strong></font></u>.  (think)

   我们的英语老师对我们非常严格,也非常友好,因此他**获得了很高的评价**。

   <font color=red><strong>is well/ highly thought of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：think well/highly of“高度评价”;该动词短语与主语our English teacher之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

7. <u><font color=red><strong>         What fun it is               </strong></font></u>to go hiking with your good friends during the holiday!（fun)

   假期期间和你的好朋友去远足是**多么开心啊**!

   <font color=red><strong>What fun it is</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：该句用了“What+a(n)十形容词十名词十主语十谓语!”这一感叹句句型结构,且 fun为不可数名词,不用冠词修饰;it在句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

8. “<u><font color=red><strong>           What about going              </strong></font></u> to Mount McKinley tomorrow?” he suggested.(what)

   “明天去麦金利山**怎么样**?”他提议。

   <font color=red><strong>What about going</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：What about doing...?“··…怎么样?”,表示提建议。</strong></font>

9. The workers in that factory complained that the money was not equally divided—some got too much while  <u><font color=red><strong>   others got too little  </strong></font></u> . (get)

   那个工厂的工人抱怨钱没有被公平地分配,一些人得到的太多,而**其他人得到的太少**。

   <font color=red><strong>others got too little</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：泛指“其他人”应用代词 others;由 got too much可知,此处应用表示相反意义的got too little.</strong></font>

10. ----Can I have a talk with you at about 5 o'clock this afternoon,Mr White?

    ----All right, I <u><font color=red><strong>          will have come back          </strong></font></u> to my office from a conference then. I will be waiting for you there.(come)

    --怀特先生,今天下午5点左右我可以和你谈谈吗?

    --好吧,那时我就**开完会**回到我的办公室了。我会在那里等你。

    <font color=red><strong>will have come back</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：表示在将来某个时间将会完成的动作应用将来完成时。</strong></font>





## lesson 25

1. "Oh, George，you don't know  <u><font color=red><strong>      how hard it is        </strong></font></u> to make ends meet,” said Jack. (hard)

   “哦,乔治,你不知道使收支平衡是**多么难**。”杰克说。

   <font color=red><strong>how hard it is</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：how引导宾语从并在从中修饰和限定hard的程度;it在从句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的不定式短语；“make ends meet”是一个常用的习语，意思是勉强维持生计或收支平衡，特别是在经济上。</strong></font>

2. It is <u><font color=red><strong>     losing his MP4 that      </strong></font></u>  makes him look so upset all these days. (lose)

   **丢失了他的 MP 4**使他这些天看起来很难过。

   <font color=red><strong>losing his MP 4 that</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：该中用了强调式“It+be十被强调部分十that...”,被强调部分为“丢失了他的 MP 4”这件事其中that不能省略;分析句子结构可知，去掉强调句式后，“丢失了他的MP 4”作主语,故应用动词- ing形式。</strong></font>

3. He has made up his mind that he will make<u><font color=red><strong>    as big a kite     </strong></font></u>as his sister had made. (big)

   他已经下了决心,他将会做一个和他姐姐做过的那个**同样大的风筝**。

   <font color=red><strong>as big a kite/a kite as big</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：此处为原级比较,结构为“...as十形容词原级+as...”,所修饰的名词位置可在该短语之前或之后。</strong></font>

4. The days <u><font color=red><strong>     that I spent       </strong></font></u>  in the countryside when I was young were the happiest time that I have ever had in my life. (spend)

   小时候**我**在乡下**度过的**那些日子是我生命中曾经拥有的最快乐的时光。

   <font color=red><strong>(that/which) I spent</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：that/which引导定语从并在从句中作宾语,可省略。</strong></font>

5. Our country  <u><font color=red><strong>    has experienced great changes    </strong></font></u> in the past thirty years,  which is the result of reform and opening-up.(experience)

   我们的国家在过去的三十年里**经历了很大的变化**,这是改革开放的结果。

   <font color=red><strong>has experienced great changes</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：由时间状语in the past thirty years可知，句子的时态应用现在完成时。</strong></font>

6. Are you going to attend the meeting <u><font color=red><strong>     to be held      </strong></font></u> in Room 2 tomorrow? (hold)

   你打算去参加明天在2号房间**召开的会议吗**?

   <font color=red><strong>to be held;that/which will be held</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：不定式作后置定语,表示将来要发生的动作;</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>也可用 that/which引导的定语从句，hold与 the meeting 之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

7. When she returned home;  she found the window opened and <u><font color=red><strong>         something stolen          </strong></font></u>. (steal)

   她回到家后,发现窗户开着,**有些东西被偷了**。

   <font color=red><strong>something stolen</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：find 后可跟动词-ed 形式作宾语补足语表示 something是steal这一动作的承受者。</strong></font>

8. The young man made so much noise that he <u><font color=red><strong>     shouldn't have been allowed       </strong></font></u> to attend the concert. (allow)

   这个年轻人制造了那么多的噪音, 他**本不该被允许**参加音乐会。

   <font color=red><strong>shouldn't have been allowed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示过去本不应该做却做了应用shouldn't have done；allow与the young man 之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

9. Linda was so angry with the letters that she <u><font color=red><strong>     tore them into pieces        </strong></font></u> and threw them into the dustbin.(tear)

   那些信件让琳达很生气, 她**把它们撕成碎片**扔进了垃圾箱。

   <font color=red><strong>tore them into pieces</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>析：tear sth into pieces“把某物撕成碎片”。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>     Take enough water      </strong></font></u>with you, otherwise you will soon suffer from thirst because it is too hot and dry these days. (take)

    你要**带上足够的水**，否则你不久就会遭受口渴之苦,因为这些天天气非常炎热和干燥。

    <font color=red><strong>Take enough water</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：分析句子结构可知，前一分为祈使句,故用动词原形。</strong></font>







## lesson 26

1. <u><font color=red><strong>     Attracted by the beauty of nature      </strong></font></u>the girl from London decided to spend another two days in the village. (attract)

   **被自然之美吸引**，这个来自伦教的女孩决定在村子里再待两天。

   <font color=red><strong>Attracted by the beauty of nature</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：逻辑主语 the girl 与attract 之间是被动关系，故用动词-ed 形式作状语，即"Attracted by the beauty of nature"在这个句子中作原因状语。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>如果使用了 "having been attracted"句子也是正确的，是过去完成进行时的被动形式，强调动作的发生在 "the girl" 决定留下之前。</strong></font>

2. In the future，we can send robots <u><font color=red><strong>     equipped with cameras       </strong></font></u> and other tools to do observation for us. (equip)

   将来,我们能发送**装有照相机的**机器人以及其他工具帮我们观察。

   <font color=red><strong>(which are) equipped with cameras</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：robots 与 equip 之间是被动关系,故用动词-ed 形式作宾语补足语;也可将该句看成定语从句,先行词是 robots,引导词在从句中作主语，故用 which,be equipped with“装有·.....”</strong></font>

3. Apples are usually <u><font color=red><strong>     sold by weight      </strong></font></u> , which is widely accepted. (sell).

   苹果通常**按重量销售**,这是被广泛接受的。

   <font color=red><strong>sold by weight</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：by“按照,根据”若其后为抽象名词,该名词前不需加冠词。</strong></font>

4. <u><font color=red><strong>      Being misunderstood      </strong></font></u> by others when you do nothing wrong at all is quite a bad experience.(misunderstand)

   根本没有做错事却**受到**别人的**误解**是个痛苦的经历。

   <font color=red><strong>Being misunderstood</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：该何缺少主语，you与misunderstand之间是被动关系，故用动词-ing 形式的被动语态。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"being done" 常用来表示一个动作正在进行且是被动的状态;"having been done"强调的是已经完成的事情对当前情况的影响</strong></font>

5. Do you want to <u><font color=red><strong>      get the dictionary delivered        </strong></font></u> to your house or would you prefer to come to the shop for it?(deliver)

   你是想要**把字典送到**你家还是愿意亲自来商店取?

   <font color=red><strong>have/get the dictionary delivered</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：have/get sth. done“使某物被做”。</strong></font>

6. So <u><font color=red><strong>     hard did I feel       </strong></font></u> it to live in an English-speaking country that I made up my mind to learn English well. (fell)

   **我觉得**生活在讲英语的国度里非常**难**以致我下定决心学好英语。

   <font color=red><strong>difficult/hard did I feel</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：so十形容词”置于句首时句子用部分倒装,句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>

7. She looks very happy.  She <u><font color=red><strong>     must have passed       </strong></font></u> the exam.

   ----她看起来很高兴。她**肯定通过了**考试。

   ----我猜是这样。考试一点都不难。

   <font color=red><strong>must have passed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示对过去情况的肯定推测应用must have done的形式。</strong></font>

8. Rather than go out for a walk, he <u><font color=red><strong>      prefers to stay       </strong></font></u> at home. (prefer)

   他**宁愿待**在家里,也不愿出去散步。

   <font color=red><strong>prefers to stay</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：prefer to do...rather than do...“宁愿做......而不愿做......”.</strong></font>

9. I wonder <u><font color=red><strong>     why he didn't do        </strong></font></u>  as he was told to. We all know that practice makes perfect. (do)

   我想知道**他为什么不**照做。我们都知道熟能生巧。

   <font color=red><strong>why he didn't do</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：why引导宾语从句，并在从句中作原因状语。wonder if 是对一般疑问句提问，例如I wonder if I could get a refund.</strong></font>

10. Professor Lee usually had them <u><font color=red><strong>        hand in     </strong></font></u> their compositions before the class was over.(hand)

    李教授通常让他们在下课之前**上交**他们的作文。

    <font color=red><strong>hand in</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：have后跟不带 to的不定式作宾语补足语;hand in“上交”;"have sb do sth"是一个常见的词组，表示让别人做某事。例如：I had my assistant send the email for me. （我让我的助手帮我发了那封邮件。）</strong></font>





## lesson 27

1. With the fog-haze weather appearing frequently, nowadays many a citizen <u><font color=red><strong>        is longing to      </strong></font></u> live where the air is fresher. (long)

   由于雾霾天气频繁出现，现在很多市民**正渴望**能生活在空气更清新的地方。

   <font color=red><strong>is longing to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：“many a+名词”作主语时谓语动词用单数形式,根据句意用现在进行时；long for（渴望、向往）、long to（渴望做某事）。</strong></font>

2. hardly <u><font color=red><strong>     did he feel      </strong></font></u> amazed when he received the admission notice from Beijing University because he thought it was the result of his efforts. (feel)

   当他收到北京大学的录取通知书时，他并没**感到**惊讶，因为他认为那是他努力的结果。

   <font color=red><strong>did he feel</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：表示否定意义的hardly置于句首时句子用部分倒装,句中为一般过去时.</strong></font>

3. But for the fact that I <u><font color=red><strong>     fastened the safety belt      </strong></font></u> in that accident, I wouldn't be alive today. (fasten)

   在那次事故中,要不是我**系了安全带**的话，我是活不到今天的。

   <font color=red><strong>fastened the safety belt</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：fasten the safety belt“系安全带”,句中为一般过去时。</strong></font>

4. The sports meet, originally <u><font color=red><strong>    due to be held      </strong></font></u> last Friday, was finally delayed because of the bad weather. (due)

   原本**定于**上周五**举行**的运动会最终由于恶劣的天气而推迟。

   <font color=red><strong>due to be held </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：due to do sth.“预定做某事”; the sports meet与 hold之间是被动关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

5. At the foot of the mountain <u><font color=red><strong>     lay a village        </strong></font></u> , where people lived a peaceful life. （lie)

   在那个山脚下**有个村庄**，那里的人们过着宁静的生活。

   <font color=red><strong>lay a village</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：介词短语at the foot of置于句首,句子用全部倒装,句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>

6. Because the wireless network is widely applied, the users surfing the Internet by cellphones is about <u><font color=red><strong>      two times as many as     </strong></font></u> those by computers. (as)

   由于无线网络的广泛应用，现在使用手机上网的用户大约是使用电脑上网的用户的**两倍多**。

   <font color=red><strong>twice/two times as many as</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：“倍数十as...as”是倍数的一种表达方式。</strong></font>

7. I am afraid that I didn't see the speed limit just now, officer. I <u><font color=red><strong>     must have been dreaming      </strong></font></u> .(dream)

   警官,恐怕我刚才没看到时速标志。我**肯定是正在开小差**。

   <font color=red><strong>must have been dreaming</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：根据句意,表示对过去正在发生的事情的肯定推测用must have been doing。</strong></font>

8. We think that special attention should be paid to <u><font color=red><strong>    practicing speaking       </strong></font></u> English in and after class. (practice)

   我们认为在课内外**练习说**英语应该得到特别的关注。

   <font color=red><strong>practicing speaking</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：pay attention to 中的to为介词,后跟动词-ing形式作宾语;practice后跟动词-ing形式作宾语。</strong></font>

9. Children under sixteen are not permitted to see such films  <u><font color=red><strong>     as are bad for     </strong></font></u> their mental development. (bad)

   16岁以下的孩子不允许看那些对他们心理发展**有害的**电影。

   <font color=red><strong>as are bad for</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：“such...as”是用来引导定语从句的短语，用于进一步说明前面提到的人或物的特征或属性。“such”是一个代词，意思是“这样的”或“那样的”，通常用来指代前面提到的事物或情况。紧随其后的“as”引出了一个比较具体的例子，用于进一步说明前面所指代的事物或情况。“such films as are bad for their mental development”是定语从句，修饰“such films”，其中“such”引导主句中的“such films”，“as”引导定语从句，意为“像……这样的电影”，“are bad for their mental development”是定语从句的谓语。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be bad for"对……有害,对……·不利”。</strong></font>

10. The head of the company promised to deal with matters of this sort <u><font color=red><strong>     the minute he returned   </strong></font></u> to his office.(minute)

    公司领导承诺**他一返回**办公室就处理这类事情。

    <font color=red><strong>the minute he returned</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：名词短语the minute可用来引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>





## lesson 28

1. My money <u><font color=red><strong>       is running out      </strong></font></u> and I have to cut down some of the living expenses. (run)

   我的钱**快要用完了**，我得削减部分生活开支了。

   <font color=red><strong>is running out</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：现在进行时可以表示将要发生的动作或状态,run out“用完,用尽”,用主动形式表示被动意义。</strong></font>

2. I think it is her personality rather than her looks <u><font color=red><strong>      that has struck         </strong></font></u> me.  Asking her to marry me is my dream. (strike)

   我想是她的个性而非她的相貌**打动了**我。让她嫁给我是我的梦想。

   <font color=red><strong>that has struck </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：strike sb.“打动某人”;此句是“It is...that...”强调句式,根据句意用现在完成时。</strong></font>

3. All the lights will be on <u><font color=red><strong>       the moment you press      </strong></font></u> the switch. (moment)

   **你一按下**开关,所有的灯都会亮。

   <font color=red><strong>the moment you press</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：the moment“-·…·就……”,引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>

4. The refrigerator that I <u><font color=red><strong>     had had repaired            </strong></font></u> broke down again. What bad luck! (repair)

   我**之前让人修理的**电冰箱又坏了。真倒霉啊!

   <font color=red><strong>had had repaired</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：have sth. done“使某物被做”,动词-ed形式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

5. My friend is crazy about the pop singer Yao Beina, He once told us,“In my mind, never <u><font color=red><strong>    have I heard     </strong></font></u> a more beautiful voice than hers. ”(hear)

   我的一个朋友对流行歌手姚贝娜痴迷不已。他曾告诉过我们:“在我心中,**我**从未**听过**比她更美的嗓音。”

   <font color=red><strong>have I heard</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：never置于句首用部分倒装。</strong></font>

6. Not <u><font color=red><strong>        informed of        </strong></font></u> the meeting notice, she was absent from the meeting. (inform)

   因未**得知**会议通知，她缺席了会议。

   <font color=red><strong>informed of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：inform of“通知”,she与 inform 之间是被动关系,故用动词-ed形式作状语。</strong></font>

7. Had it not been for my respectable teacher Susan, I <u><font color=red><strong>     wouldn't be sitting       </strong></font></u> in the bright and spacious office now.(sit)

   如果不是因为我那可敬的苏珊老师,此刻我**就不会正坐在**宽敞明亮的办公室里了。

   <font color=red><strong>wouldn't be sitting</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：条件句表示与过去事实相反的假设，主句表示与现在事实相反的假设,故主句谓语动词用“would+动词原形”的形式,根据句意用现在进行时。</strong></font>

8. Jack is often educated by his parents to be friendly to others even if <u><font color=red><strong>      (he is) unfairly treated       </strong></font></u>.(treat)

   杰克的父母经常教育他对人要友善,即使是**受到了不公平的对待**。

   <font color=red><strong>(he is) unfairly treated</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：even if引导的是让步状语从句, he与treat之间是被动关系,故用被动语态;主从句主语一致,且含有be动词,故可以省略“主语+be”的形式。</strong></font>

9. It <u><font color=red><strong>    never occurred to         </strong></font></u> him that he would be reduced to such a sorry state.（occur)

   他**从未想到过**自己会沦落到如此境地。

   <font color=red><strong>never occurred to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：it occurs to sb.“某人想到”。</strong></font>

10. Since the foreigner came,  we have been giving her Chinese lessons  <u><font color=red><strong>       in exchange for       </strong></font></u> her teaching us English.(exchange)

    自从那个外国人来了之后,我们就一直教她汉语来**作为**她教我们英语的**交换**。

    <font color=red><strong>in exchange for</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：in exchange for“作为交换,以换取”。</strong></font>





# part 05

## lesson 29

1. Every possible means <u><font color=red><strong>       has been used         </strong></font></u> to prevent the air pollution, but the sky is still not clear. (use)

   所有可能的防治空气污染的方法**都用了**，但天空还是不晴朗。

   <font color=red><strong>has been used</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由every修饰的名词作主语时,谓语动词用单数形式, means与 use之间是被动关系,故用被动语态,根据句意用现在完成时。</strong></font>

   1. **means**

      **"Means" 可以是一个名词，表示手段、方法或工具等意思。means的复数形式是means。该词在单数和复数形式上拼写相同。**

      - **He has several means of transportation.(他有几种交通工具)**
      - **The means of transportation in this city are buses, trains, and taxis.(这个城市的交通方式有公共汽车、火车和出租车。)**
      - **I don't have the means to buy a new car. (我没有买新车的资本)**

      **mean的一些常见意思**

      - **意味着，表明 例句：What does this word mean?**
      - **意欲，打算 例句：I mean to finish this project by the end of the week.**
      - **想要，需要 例句：I meant to ask you if you could help me with something.**

   2. **prevent**

      **prevent是一个动词，意思是阻止、预防、避免。它通常用于描述采取措施或行动以防止某种情况的发生，或防止某人做某事。例如：**

      - **Wearing a mask can help prevent the spread of COVID-19.**

   3. **clear**

      **"clear" 是一个多义词，可以表示以下意思：**

      1. **清晰的，明显的（adjective）**
      2. **清空，清理（verb）**
      3. **使消除，消除（verb）**
      4. **明确的，确定的（adjective）**
      5. **畅通的，通畅的（adjective）**
      6. **完全的，彻底的（adjective）**
      7. **显然，毫无疑问（adverb）**

2. To his great surprise, no sooner <u><font color=red><strong>        had he ended             </strong></font></u> his speech than thunderous applause broke out.(end)

   令他十分惊讶的是，**他**的演讲刚**结束**就响起了雷鸣般的掌声。

   <font color=red><strong>had he ended/put an end to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>no sooner. . . than...“一...….就……",no sooner后的句子中用过去完成时。</strong></font>

   1. **thunderous   adj. 雷鸣般的;声音很大的;怒容满面的;面色阴沉的;怒气冲冲的**
   2. **applause       n.掌声;鼓掌;喝彩**

3. Those successful deaf dancers think that dancing is an activity <u><font color=red><strong>     in which eyesight matters         </strong></font></u> more than hearing.(matter)

   那些成功的聋人舞者认为，舞蹈是一种视力比听力**更重要的**活动。

   <font color=red><strong>where/in which eyesight matters</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>定语从句的先行词是activity,引导词在从句中作地点状语,故用 where,相当于in which.</strong></font>

   1. **matter**

      **作为名词，"matter"的意思可以有以下几种：**

      1. **物质，物质实体**
      2. **事情，事件，问题**
      3. **重要性，关系，意义**

      **例如：**

      - **Chemistry deals with the study of matter.（化学研究物质。）**
      - **We need to discuss this matter further.（我们需要进一步讨论这个问题。）**
      - **Money isn't the only matter in life.（金钱并不是生活中唯一重要的事情。）**

      **作为形容词，"matter"的意思可以是“有重要性的”或“有关系的”。例如：**

      - **It's a matter of life and death.（这关系到生死。）**
      - **This is a matter of great concern to us.（这对我们非常重要。）**

   2. **deaf** 

      **adj. 聋的;失聪的;对…充耳不闻的，不愿听的，不注意的，不依从的**
      **vt. 使聋，使听不见**

4. <u><font color=red><strong>      That he was not invited         </strong></font></u>to the conference surprised us，since he was an important figure in this field after all.(invite)

   **他没有被邀请**参加会议很让我们吃惊,因为毕竟他是这一领域的重要人物。

   <font color=red><strong>That he was not invited/His not being invited</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>主语从句中that不作任何成分,也没有任何意义, he与 invite 之间是被动关系,故用被动语态,根据句意用一般过去时;也可看成是动名词的独立主格结构。</strong></font>

   after all：毕竟;终究

5. The car ran down the hill,  and the driver was reported,  according to the local newspaper,  <u><font color=red><strong>     to have been killed       </strong></font></u> in the accident(kill)

   车从山上滚了下来,据当地报纸报道，司机在这场事故中**丧生了**。

   <font color=red><strong>to have been killed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be reported to do“据报道做某事”, kill表示的动作发生在 was reported表示的动作之前,故用不定式的完成式,且he与kill之间是被动关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

6. Create your own map of your goal. Keep it <u><font color=red><strong>       where you can see          </strong></font></u> it daily, so that you do not forget where you are going. (see)

   为自己的目标制作一张地图。放在每天**你能看到的地方**，这样你就不会忘记你要去往何处。

   <font color=red><strong>where you can see</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由句意知缺少地点状语,故用 where引导地点状语从句。</strong></font>

7. But for your timely encouragement, I <u><font color=red><strong>        would have lost heart       </strong></font></u> after going through so much difficulty. (lose)

   要不是你的及时鼓励，经历这么多的困难之后我**就灰心**了。

   <font color=red><strong>would have lost heart</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>but for表示的条件是与过去事实相反的假设,主句谓语动词用would have done的形式。</strong></font>

   1. **lose heart**

      **意思是失去信心或动力，感到沮丧或气馁。常用于描述在困难或挫折面前感到无助或放弃的情况，例如："Don't lose heart. Keep trying, and you'll eventually succeed."（不要失去信心，继续尝试，你最终会成功的。）**

   2. **encouragement**

      **n.鼓舞;鼓励;起激励作用的事物**

   3. **encourage**

      **vt.支持;鼓励;激励;鼓动;劝告;怂恿;促进;助长;刺激**

   4. **courage**

      **n.勇气;勇敢;无畏;胆量**

8. Success is not final，and failure is not fatal;  it is the courage to continue <u><font color=red><strong>       that really counts         </strong></font></u>. (count)

   成功不是结局，失败并非毁灭；**真正重要的**是要有勇气继续前进。

   <font color=red><strong>that really counts</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句式“It is...that...”。</strong></font>

   1. **count**

      - **v.计数;(按顺序)数数;**

      - **n.总数;数出总数;**

      - **有重要性 matter**

        **Every point in this game counts.（这场比赛每一分都很重要。）**

   2. **fatal**

      **adj.致命的;灾难性的;毁灭性的;导致失败的**

9. ---Catherine,I have cleaned the room for you.

   ---Thanks. You <u><font color=red><strong>     needn't have cleaned       </strong></font></u> it. I could manage it myself. (clean)

   -----凯瑟琳,我已经帮你打扫了房间。

   -----谢谢。你**本不必打扫的**。我自己能行。

   <font color=red><strong>needn't have cleaned</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示过去本没有必要做却做了，应用needn't have done的形式。</strong></font>

10. Despite all the fame Tom Hanks has gained as a movie star,  he <u><font color=red><strong>    has an appetite for      </strong></font></u> further success in his art career. (appetite)

    作为一名影星,尽管汤姆·汉克斯已经有了这么大的名气，他还是有在艺术生涯中进一步成功**的欲望**。

    <font color=red><strong>has an appetite for </strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>have an appetite for“对·……有欲望”。</strong></font>
    
    1. **despite**
    
       **prep.即使;尽管;尽管(自己)不愿意**
       **n.怨恨;恶意;轻蔑;侮辱**
    
    2. **gain**
    
       **v.获得;赢得;**
    
       **n.(尤指财富、重量的)增值，增加;**





## lesson 30

1. <u><font color=red><strong>        Being opposed          </strong></font></u>to teaching children about drug only reminds them of its existence, which is a very dangerous approach. (oppose)

   **反对**把毒品知识教给小孩只会引起他们注意到它的存在，这是一个很危险的方法。

   <font color=red><strong>Being opposed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>句子缺少主语,且逻辑主语与oppose之间是被动关系,故用动词-ing形式的被动语态。</strong></font>

2. Many new technologies，such as Google Glasses,  3D printing,  and cloud computing,  <u><font color=red><strong>      have been effecting        </strong></font></u> our lives in the past five years. (affect)

   在过去的五年里，许多新科技像谷歌眼镜3D打印、云计算，**一直在影响着**我们的生活。

   <font color=red><strong>have been affecting</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>such as后面的成分是主语 many new technologies的同位语,谓语动词的形式由主语而定,由时间状语in the past five years及句意可知,用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

3. Research finds that social network users have more than <u><font color=red><strong>       twice as many friends      </strong></font></u> online as in real life. (as)

   研究发现社交网络用户在网络上拥有的**朋友**是现实生活中的**两倍多**。

   <font color=red><strong>twice as many friends</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“……是…的两倍”用“twice as. .. as...”。</strong></font>

4. If the old fashioned museum hadn't been destroyed a decade ago, people there <u><font color=red><strong>       could visit        </strong></font></u> it as a place of interest now. (visit)

   如果那个老博物馆十年前没被毁，那儿的人们现在就**能**把它当作名胜**游览**了。

   <font color=red><strong>could visit</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句为错综时间条件句,条件句表示与过去事实相反的假设,主句表示与现在事实相反,故主句谓语动词用“could十动词原形”。</strong></font>

5. <u><font color=red><strong>      Shortly after you left      </strong></font></u><u><font color=red><strong>               </strong></font></u><u><font color=red><strong>               </strong></font></u>，a man came into the office looking for you.(shortly)

   **在你离开后不久**，一个男人到办公室来找你。

   <font color=red><strong>Shortly after you left</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>after引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>

6. The village <u><font color=red><strong>    where I grew up     </strong></font></u> is a very beautiful place in the mountains. (grow)

   那是一个非常美丽的山村，**我从小在那里长大**。

   <font color=red><strong>where/in which I grew up</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>where引导定语从句,并在从句中作地点状语,先行词是 village,此处 where相当于in which;grow up“长大”,是发生在过去的动作,故用一般过去时。</strong></font>

7. We'll set out next Monday. It is important that you <u><font color=red><strong>     (should) get everything ready     </strong></font></u> on Saturday. (ready)

   我们下周一出发。周六你**要把一切准备好**，这很重要。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) get everything ready</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>It is/was important that...中that从句应用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should＋动词原形”,should可省略;get后可跟形容词作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

8. They realize that it is <u><font color=red><strong>     of great value     </strong></font></u> to teach the languages to the younger generation. (value)

   他们认识到教年轻一代学 习语言是**很有价值的**。

   <font color=red><strong>of great value</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"of+名词”相当于该名词相对应的形容词，of great value“很有价值的”,相当于 valuable.</strong></font>

9. By the time you arrive home，I <u><font color=red><strong>       will be sleeping    </strong></font></u>，so please don't make any noise when you come in. (sleep)

   你到家的时候我**将正在睡觉**，所以你进来的时候请不要弄出声。

   <font color=red><strong>will/shall be sleeping</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示将来某个时间正在进行的动作应用将来进行时。</strong></font>

10. The question <u><font color=red><strong>     why they choose     </strong></font></u>to live in the countryside but to work in the city nowadays is still under discussion. (choose)

    如今**他们为什么选择**在乡下居住而在城里工作这个问题仍在讨论中。

    <font color=red><strong>why they choose</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>why引导同位语从句,用来解释说明question的内容,并在从句中作原因状语。</strong></font>





## lesson 31

1. The phrase ，"Let's be friends, tuhao!"  set off a language shock , <u><font color=red><strong>    which originally appeared in       </strong></font></u> an online conversation.(appear)

   “土豪,我们做朋友吧!”这句话引发了一场语言震撼，**它最初出现在**一个网络对话里。

   <font color=red><strong>which first/originally appeared in</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句为非限制性定语从句,先行词是“Let's be friends,tuhao!”,引导词在从句中作主语，用 which,根据语境可知发生在过去,故用一般过去时。</strong></font>

2. <u><font color=red> <strong>    Champion as he is          </strong></font></u> ，Sun Yang has been arrested for driving without a license. (as)

   **虽然是冠军**, 孙杨还是由于无证驾驶被警方拘留。

   <font color=red><strong>Champion as he/Sun Yang is</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>as引导让步状语从句时,从句中的表语需提到句首,且表语若是单数名词还要去掉冠词。</strong></font>

   **"Without" 是一个介词，表示 "没有" 或 "不带有" 的意思**

   1. **Without + 名词，表示某物或某人的缺乏或没有：**
      - **Without money, you can't buy anything.（没有钱，你什么都买不到）**
      - **I can't cook without a recipe.(没有菜谱我就不会做饭)**
   2. **Without + 动词-ing，表示在某种情况下的缺乏或不具备：**
      - **Without sleeping enough, you'll feel tired all day.(睡眠不足，你会觉得一整天都很累。)**
      - **Without speaking, he left the room.(他一声不吭地离开了房间。)**
   3. **Without + to + 动词原形，表示做某事时不需要采取某种行动：**
      - **You can learn a lot without going to college.（你不用上大学就能学到很多东西）**
      - **You can finish the task without staying up all night.（你可以在不熬夜的情况下完成任务。）**
   4. **Without + that，表示某个动作可以在某种情况下省略：**
      - **He answered the question without that he knew the answer.(他回答了这个问题，却不知道答案。)**

   **注意：Without 也可以作为介词使用，后面接名词或动名词，表示没有某种物品或行动。例如：He walked to the office without a coat. (没有穿外套)**

3. <u><font color=red><strong>      Put what you want       </strong></font></u> in the"shopping cart", and you can make a list of potential purchases and avoid purchasing on impulse. (put)

   **把你想要的放到**“购物车”中，你就可以生成一个购物清单，以避免冲动购物。

   <font color=red><strong>Put what you want/Put everything (that）you want</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>put后可以跟宾语从句也可以跟定语从句,跟宾语从句时引导词用what，跟定语从句时引导词用that，that可以省略。</strong></font>

   **purchases ：n.所购物；获得物（purchase 的复数）**

   **purchase : n.购买;采购;购买的东西;**

   **potential ：adj.潜在的;可能的；n.可能性;潜在性;潜力;潜质;电位;电势;电压**

   **avoid doing something ：避免做某事。例如：I always avoid eating too much junk food.**

   **impulse ：n.推动，驱使;冲力；v.推动，促进；adj.一时兴起的，随兴的**

   **"On impulse" 意为“冲动地”，表示在一时冲动下做某事，没有经过深思熟虑。例如：I bought that shirt on impulse, but I regret it now. （我当时冲动地买了那件衬衫，但现在后悔了。）**

4. The air pollution in China is so serious that only when all departments take effective measures<u><font color=red><strong>        can we reduce          </strong></font></u>damage hopefully. (reduce)

   中国的空气污染如此严重，只有所有部门都采取有效措施**我们**才有望**减少**危害。

   <font color=red><strong>can/will we reduce</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>only修饰的状语置于句首时,主句部分用部分倒装。</strong></font>

   1. **effective ：adj.有效的;产生预期结果的;实际的;事实上的;生效的;起作用的**

      - **<font color=red>effective for 对…有效</font>**
      - <font color=red>**effective date 生效日期；有效日期**</font>
      - <font color=red>**effective from 从开始生效;生效日期 (The new speed limit on this road becomes effective from 1 June.这条路上新的限速规定自6月1日起生效。 )**</font>

   2. **take measure :采取措施 (We must <font color=red>take measure to protect</font> the crops from insect pests. 我们必须采取措施保护庄稼，使之不受虫害。)**

   3. **damage ：n.(有形的)损坏，破坏，损失;  vt.损害;伤害;毁坏;破坏**

   4. **当表示上升或增长时，常用的词语有：**

      1. **increase：增加、增长 例如：The number of visitors to the park <font color=red>increased</font> by 20% this year.（公园的游客数量今年增长了20%。）**
      2. **rise：上升、升高 例如：The price of gasoline <font color=red>has risen</font> sharply in recent weeks.（近几周，汽油价格急剧上涨。）**
      3. **grow：增加、生长 例如：The company has <font color=red>grown</font> rapidly since its founding.（自创立以来，该公司发展迅速。）**
      4. **climb：攀升、上升 例如：The temperature <font color=red>climbed</font> to 90 degrees in the afternoon.（下午气温攀升到了90度。）**

      **当表示下降或减少时，常用的词语有：**

      1. **decrease：减少、降低 例如：The amount of rainfall in the region <font color=red>decreased</font> significantly this year.（该地区的降雨量今年明显减少。）**
      2. **fall：下降、跌落 例如：The stock market <font color=red>fell</font> sharply yesterday.（昨天股市大跌。）**
      3. **decline：下降、衰退 例如：The sales of the company have <font color=red>declined</font> over the past few months.（公司的销售额在过去几个月里有所下降。）**
      4. **drop：下降、降低 例如：The temperature is expected to <font color=red>drop</font> below freezing tonight.（预计今晚气温会降到冰点以下。）**
      5. **reduce 表示减少的动词，可以用来描述数量、价值、质量等的降低。We need to <font color=red>reduce</font> the amount of waste we produce.**

      <font color=red>**注意，这些词语可以互换使用，但有时候用法有所不同。例如，increase和grow都表示增长，但grow更常用于生物学或植物方面的增长，而increase则更常用于数量、大小、规模等方面的增长。**</font>

5. <u><font color=red><strong>       It has been reported       </strong></font></u>in the Wall Street Journal that Apple has already asked its suppliers to increase production of the gold model iPhone 5s to meet the market demand. (report)

   《华尔街日报》**已经报道**，苹果公司已经通知供货方增加生产金色的iPhone 5s以满足市场需求。

   <font color=red><strong>It has been reported</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it is reported“据报道”,根据句意用现在完成时。</strong></font>

   1. **Journal ：n.杂志;日记;日志;(某学科或专业的)报纸;刊物;**

   2. **Journey ：n.旅行;(尤指长途)行程**

   3. **demand ：n.需要;所需之物; v.需要;强烈要求**

   4. **recommend ：v.推荐;举荐;介绍;劝告;建议;使显得吸引人;使受欢迎**

   5. **表示“提供，供给”的几个常见动词有：**

      1. **provide：提供，供应，是最常用的一个词，通常用于正式、书面的场合。**

         **例句：The hotel provides complimentary breakfast for its guests. (酒店为客人提供免费早餐。)**

      2. **supply：供给，提供，也是比较常用的一个词，多用于口语或者商务场合。**

         **例句：The store supplies fresh vegetables every morning. (这家店每天早上提供新鲜蔬菜。)**

      3. **offer：提供，提议，有时也可以表示“出售”。**

         **例句：The company is offering free samples of their new product. (这家公司正在提供他们新产品的免费样品。)**

      4. **furnish：提供，供应，通常用于正式场合。**

         **例句：The apartment is fully furnished with everything you need. (这间公寓配备了你所需要的一切。)**

      5. **cater：提供餐饮服务，满足需求。**

         **例句：The restaurant caters to all dietary requirements. (这家餐厅满足所有饮食需求。)**

      6. **dispense：提供，分配，通常用于医疗、法律等专业场合。**

         **例句：The pharmacist dispensed the medication as prescribed by the doctor. (药剂师按照医生的处方提供了药物。)**

      **需要注意的是，这些动词有时会存在细微的差别，具体使用时需要根据语境和场合灵活运用。**

6. I should have attended your party, but I <u><font color=red><strong>      was busy preparing for       </strong></font></u>an examination yesterday. (prepare)

   我本应该来参加你的聚会的,但是我昨天**忙着准备**一场考试。

   <font color=red><strong>was busy (in) preparing for</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be busy in doing sth.“忙着做某事”, in可以省略。</strong></font>

7. A latest study shows that <u><font color=red><strong>     being exposed to     </strong></font></u>the natural sunlight for a few minutes a day helps to reduce the risk of getting cancer. (expose)

   最新研究表明每天**晒**几分钟太阳有助于减少得癌症的风险.

   <font color=red><strong>being exposed to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>句子缺少主语,用动词-ing形式,且主语“人们”与expose之间是被动关系,故用动词-ing形式的被动式。</strong></font>

8. I really don't know<u><font color=red><strong>    why it is that    </strong></font></u>he is late for school every day. (it)

   我真的不知道他**到底为什么**天天上学迟到。

   <font color=red><strong>why it is that</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句的特殊疑问句式“疑问词十is it+that...”,根据句意疑问词用 why,且宾语从句中用陈述语序。</strong></font>

   be late for ：v.迟到

9. China, our motherland, is<u><font color=red><strong>     one of the largest countries     </strong></font></u>in the world, with a population of more than 1.3 billion.(large)

   中国，我们的祖国，有着13多亿人口，是世界上**最大的国家之一**。

   <font color=red><strong>one of the largest countries</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"最大的"暗示应用形容词最高级形式，表示“……之一”的 one of后应跟可数名词复数形式。</strong></font>

10. Seeing that the workers' attitude toward the work was not that serious,  the manager required that they<u><font color=red><strong>    (should)finish it   </strong></font></u>ahead of time. (finish)

    看到工人们的工作态度不是那么认真，经理便要求他们提前**完成**。

    <font color=red><strong>(should) finish it</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>非谓语作状语的句型，一般都是有一个逗号把一句话分成两个半句话，其中半句有正常的主语、谓语和宾语，这个正常的主谓宾可以写在前半句也可以写在后半句。</strong></font>
    <font color=red><strong>然后另外的半句是非谓语开头，并且这个非谓语动词表示的动作就是另半句完整的主谓宾句子中的主语“主动做的”或者“被做”或者“将要去做”。</strong></font>
    <font color=red><strong>也有可能就是完整的一整句话。</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>Seeing the police, he made a run for the exit. Seeing为现在分词作时间状语，例如：Seeing the police, he made a run for the exit.(当看到警察(时)，他就向出口奔去。</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>可以改为 When seeing the police, he made a run for the exit.改为正常结构为When he saw the police, he made a run for the exit.</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>require“要求”,其后跟宾语从句时从句中用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should十动词原形”,should可省略。</strong></font>
    
    **"toward" 是一个介词，表示朝向、对于、关于的意思。它可以用来表示方向、趋势、倾向、感情等方面，常见的用法包括：**
    
    1. **表示方向：朝向某个方向，例如 "He walked toward the park" （他走向公园）。**
    2. **表示趋势：指向某个目标、目的，例如 "She is working toward her goal" （她正在为实现自己的目标而努力）。**
    3. **表示倾向：表示某种态度或看法，例如 "I'm leaning toward accepting the job offer" （我倾向于接受这个工作机会）。**
    4. **表示感情：表示某种情感或感觉，例如 "She is hostile toward him" （她对他怀有敌意）。**
    
    **注意，"toward" 还有一个变体 "towards"，两者用法基本相同，只是在美式英语中更常见使用 "toward"，而在英式英语中更常使用 "towards"。此外，"toward" 还可以作为副词使用，表示朝向的方向或目标前进，例如 "The car drove toward the mountains"（车子向着山脉行驶）**





## lesson 32

1. A cook will be immediately fired if he <u><font color=red><strong>    is found smoking     </strong></font></u> in the kitchen. (find)

   如果一个厨师**被发现**在厨房**抽烟**，他就会立即被开除。

   <font color=red><strong>is found smoking</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>find后可跟动词-ing形式作宾语补足语，表示 he是正在进行的smoke这一动作的发出者;find与 he之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用被动语态。(主将从现)</strong></font>

   **"发现某人在某事"可以翻译为"discover someone in something"，也可以使用"catch someone in something"，其中"catch"的意思是"捕捉"，在此引申为"发现"；"Find someone in something"通常指在某个地方或某种情况下找到某人，而不是发现某人正在做某事。**

2. <u><font color=red><strong>      With the help of        </strong></font></u> the telephone, people can keep in touch with anyone at any time and in any place for urgent help. (help)

   **在**电话**的帮助下**，人们可以随时随地联系任何人来紧急救助。

   <font color=red><strong>With the help of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>with the help of“在…·…的帮助下”。"Under" 通常表示在某个权威或控制之下，或者是在某个物体或表面之下。因此，"在......的帮助下" 通常不用 "under"。使用 "with the help of" 或 "with the assistance of" 是更常见和自然的表达方式。</strong></font>

3. The best of all is <u><font color=red><strong>    that computers can tell      </strong></font></u> me almost everything I want to know. (tell)

   最棒的是**计算机能告诉**我几乎所有我想知道的事。

   <font color=red><strong>that computers can tell</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导表语从句,在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略。</strong></font>

   - <font color=red><strong>the best of all：最好的</strong></font>
   - <font color=red><strong>the worst of all：最糟糕的</strong></font>

4. The best part <u><font color=red><strong>   given to   </strong></font></u> Peter，John was so disappointed that he felt unwilling to continue his taking part in the play. (give)

   最好的角色**给了**彼得,约翰如此失望以至于他不愿继续参加这个演出了。

   <font color=red><strong>given to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>前后两分句的主语不一致,且没有连接词连接,故用独立主格结构,同时give与 the best part 之间为逻辑上的动宾关系,故用动词-ed形式;give sth. to sb.“给某人某物”。</strong></font>

   **"Continue doing sth" 的意思是继续做某事，其中的"continue"表示持续，延续某种状态或动作，"doing sth"表示正在进行某项活动或任务。**

   **"take part in"的意思是“参加，参与”。常用于表示某人参与某项活动或事件，如“take part in a meeting”（参加会议）、“take part in a competition”（参加比赛）等。**

5. Ever since the sheep Dolly was cloned in 1997，his phone <u><font color=red><strong>        has been ringing         </strong></font></u> with people calling in hopes of making the copies of their pets." (ring)

   自从1997年多利羊被克隆之后，他的电话就**一直响个不停**，人们希望自己的宠物也被克隆。

   <font color=red><strong>has been ringing</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由时间状语ever since可知,应用现在完成时,且这一动作目前还在进行,故用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

   **"in hopes of"是一个固定短语，意思是"希望达成某事"或"期望实现某事"，通常用于表达期望或愿望，常用于正式的或文学性的语言。例如："I am studying hard in hopes of getting a scholarship."（我正在努力学习，希望能获得奖学金。）**

6. There was a lot of fun at yesterday's party. You <u><font color=red><strong>     should have came       </strong></font></u> ,but why didn't you? (come)

   昨天的聚会很好玩。你**本应该来的**,但是你为什么没来?

   <font color=red><strong>should have come</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示过去本应该做却未做,应用 should have done.</strong></font>

7. Her story tells us that we should value <u><font color=red><strong>   what we have    </strong></font></u> and try our best to overcome any difficulty in life. (have)

   她的故事告诉我们应当珍惜**我们所拥有的**，并且尽力克服生活中的任何困难。

   <font color=red><strong>what we have</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>what引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语。</strong></font>

   1. **try one's best to**

      **"try one's best to" 是一个表达竭尽全力去做某事的短语。通常用于描述一个人非常努力地尝试达成某个目标或完成某项任务，表达一种努力争取成功的决心和行动。例如：I will try my best to finish the project before the deadline.（我将尽力在截止日期前完成这个项目。）**

   2. **had better do**

      **"had better do"是一种建议或警告，意思是"最好做某事"或"最好不要做某事，否则会有不好的后果"。它常常用来向别人提出一些建议或者警告，表示某种行为或决定是最好的选择，或者是为了避免某种不良后果而需要遵循的建议。**

      **例如：You had better study hard for the exam if you want to pass it.（如果你想通过考试，最好努力学习。）**

8. In my opinion, the best way to show love is <u><font color=red><strong>      to get ready to help         </strong></font></u> people who are in trouble, no matter whether they are family members or strangers. (ready)

   在我看来,表达爱的最好方式就是**准备好帮助**处于困境中的人们，无论他们是你的家人还是陌生人。

   <font color=red><strong>to get/be ready to help</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>不定式作表语,表示主语的职责等;get/be ready to do sth.“准备好做某事”</strong></font>

9. My mother, a middle school teacher, has a pair of keen eyes <u><font color=red><strong>     that can speak          </strong></font></u> .(speak)

   我的母亲是一位中学教师，她有一双敏锐的、**会说话的**眼睛。

   <font color=red><strong>which/that can speak</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>which/that引导定语从句,并在从句中作主语,不能省略。</strong></font>

10. Now the number of the students and teachers in this primary school <u><font color=red><strong>       adds up to      </strong></font></u> over 2 000. (add)

    现在这所小学的师生人数**总共**两千多。

    <font color=red><strong>adds up to</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>"the number of＋可数名词复数”作主语时,谓语动词用单数形式; add up to“总计,总共”。</strong></font>

##  lesson 33

1. With the 2010 World Cup a distant memory,  the country is doing,  <u><font color=red><strong>     what she can to         </strong></font></u> bid for the 2022 World Cup. (what)

   随着2010年世界杯已坠人史册，这个国家正**尽她切所能去**申办2022年世界杯。

   <font color=red><strong>what she can to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>doing后是宾语从句, to bid for...表示目的。</strong></font>

2. <u><font color=red><strong>         Dating from       </strong></font></u> the Spring and Autumn and the Warring States, the Great Wall is still perfectly preserved. (date)

   **追溯到**春秋战国时代，长城至今仍保存完好。

   <font color=red><strong>Dating from/back to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>date from/back to“追溯到”; the Great Wall 与date之间是主动关系,故用动词-ing形式作状语；句首的非谓语动词是"dating"，它是作时间状语，表示时间的起点，修饰"the Great Wall"。</strong></font>

   **preserve ：vt.保护;维护;保留;n.(某人或群体活动、工作等的)专门领域;**

3. At the airport,  we saw Lady Gaga,  the famous super star,  <u><font color=red><strong>     alongside whom were         </strong></font></u> several bodyguards.(alongside)

   在机场，我们见到了Lady Caga这位著名的超级巨星。**她旁边有**几位保镖。

   <font color=red><strong>alongside whom were</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为“介词十关系代词”引导的非限制性定语从句,其先行词是Lady Gaga,故用alongside whom.</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>这句话中的非限制性定语从句是“the famous super star, alongside whom were several bodyguards”。这个定语从句修饰先行词“Lady Gaga”，用逗号和主句隔开，不是必需的信息，但可以提供额外的描述。其中，关系代词“whom”在定语从句中作为介词“alongside”的宾语，并且指代先行词“Lady Gaga”。</strong></font>

4. <u><font color=red><strong>    Being fed up with     </strong></font></u> sitting in the classroom all day may account for these students dropping out. (fed)

   **厌倦了**整日坐在教室里可能是这些学生辍学的原因。

   <font color=red><strong>Being fed up with</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be fed up with“厌倦”,students 与 fed之间是主动关系,故用动词-ing形式。“Being fed up with sitting in the classroom all day”是原因状语，解释了为什么这些学生辍学，因此是原因状语；"dropping out"在这个句子中是动词现在分词作结果状语。它说明了“这些学生退学的原因”是因为他们对整天坐在教室里感到厌烦。</strong></font>

   **account for ：导致，解释（某种事实或情况）;解释，说明（某事）;**

   **drop out ：退学;退出（比赛等）;**

5. But for his sudden departure, our plan <u><font color=red><strong>    would have paid off         </strong></font></u>.(pay)

   要不是他的突然离去，我们的计划**就成功了**。

   <font color=red><strong>would have paid off</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>but for表示的是与过去事实相反的假设,故句子的谓语动词用 would have done的形式。</strong></font>

   **“pay off”是一个常用的短语，通常用来指付清债务或取得成功等意义。**

   - **还清债务：这是“pay off”最常见的用法，表示完成还款。例如：“I finally paid off my student loans after ten years of payments.”（我终于在十年的还款后还清了我的学生贷款。）**
   - **取得成功：这个意思可以指通过付出努力得到回报，也可以指完成一个计划或目标。例如：“All his hard work paid off when he got the promotion.”（当他得到晋升时，他的所有辛勤工作都得到了回报。）**

6. Believe it or not, Mr Smith is said <u><font color=red><strong>      to have applied for        </strong></font></u>the position three times up till now. (apply)

   信不信由你，据说迄今为止史密斯先生**已经申请**这个职位三次了。

   <font color=red><strong>to have applied for</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be said to do sth.“据说做某事”, apply表示的动作发生在过去动作be said之前,故用不定式的完成式;apply for“申请……”。</strong></font>

7. The chief engineer including his colleagues <u><font color=red><strong>    has been betraying    </strong></font></u> state secrets to America over these  years.(betray)

   这些年来，这位总工程师与他的同事们**一直**在向美国**泄露**国家机密。

   <font color=red><strong>has been betraying</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>主语后带有including短语时,谓语动词仍与主语保持一致,此处用单数形式,根据句意“泄露国家机密”是一直在进行的事情,故用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

   **chief ：n.(公司或机构的)最高领导人;首领; adj.主要的;最重要的;首要的;**

   **chef ：n.厨师;(尤指餐馆、饭店等的)主厨，厨师长**

8. I don't know <u><font color=red><strong>    why it was     </strong></font></u> that our headmaster was absent from such an important meeting.(why)

   我不知道我们的校长**到底为什么**缺席如此重要的会议。

   <font color=red><strong>why it was</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句的特殊疑问句式,且宾语从句中用陈述语序。</strong></font>

   headmaster ：n.(尤指私立学校的)校长

9. There <u><font color=red><strong>    being no modern equipment    </strong></font></u> then, they had to build their defense works by hand. (equipment) 

   **因为**那时**没有现代化的设备**，所以他们不得不人工建造他们的防御工事。

   <font color=red><strong>being no modern equipment</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为独立主格结构,逻辑主语与be之间是主动关系,故用动词-ing形式；在这个句子中，“There being no modern equipment then”是一个独立主格结构。其中，“there”是形式主语，实际上并不承担语义角色。而“being no modern equipment then”则是现在分词短语，作为主语补语，修饰形式主语“there”。整个结构与主句“they had to build their defense works by hand”并列，并且可以独立成为一个完整的句子，意为“当时没有现代设备”。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>      It will be eight months       </strong></font></u> before we leave school and go to university. (month)

    **八个月后**，我们就离开学校上大学了。
    
    <font color=red><strong>It will be eight months</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>句式“It will be+一段时间＋before...”表示“多长时间之后”。</strong></font>
    
    **“It will be+一段时间+before...”的结构中，“It”是一个形式主语，用于占据句子主语的位置，表示强调后面的主语。“will be”则表示未来将会发生的情况。“一段时间”可以是具体的时间长度，例如“a week”或“a month”，也可以是抽象的时间概念，例如“a long time”或“a while”。最后，“before”后面接的部分表示具体需要等待的事情或目标。例如，“It will be a few months before we can move into our new house.”（我们要等几个月才能搬进新房子。）**





## lesson 34

1. He has made a promise to his boss <u><font color=red><strong>    that he will return          </strong></font></u> in three days as long as he can get to the destination in time. (return)

   他向他老板承诺只要他能及时到达目的地**就将**三天后**回来**。

   <font color=red><strong>that he will return </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导的同位语从句解释说明promise的内容。</strong></font>

   **"as long as" 是一个短语，意思是 "只要"，"长达"，"一直"，"在...期间"。通常用来表达条件、时间、程度等方面的限定。例如：**

   - **As long as you study hard, you will pass the exam.（只要你努力学习，你会通过考试。）**
   - **I will support you as long as it takes.（我会一直支持你。）**
   - **You can stay here as long as you like.（你可以在这里呆多久都可以。）**

2. It has been announced in the media <u><font color=red><strong>    that the president will visit     </strong></font></u> our school this May. (visit)

   **这位总统将于**今年五月**访问**我校,这在媒体上已经公布了。

   <font color=red><strong>that the president will visit</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it为形式主语,真正的主语是后面的that从句.</strong></font>

   **announce ：v.宣布;宣告(决定、计划等);**

3. When I arrived home, I found <u><font color=red><strong>    my watch stolen    </strong></font></u> which made me a little upset. (steal)

   当我到家时,我发现**我的手表被偷了**,这让我有点伤心。

   <font color=red><strong>(that） my watch had been stolen/my watch stolen</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>found后可以看成是宾语从句,引导词that可以省略;也可以看成是find sth. done“发现某物被做”。</strong></font>

4. As it turned out to be a small house party, we <u><font color=red><strong>      needn't have dressed up         </strong></font></u> so formally. (dress)

   结果这是一场小型的家庭聚会,我们**没有必要着装**这么正式。

   <font color=red><strong>needn't have dressed up</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>needn't have done“本没有必要做某事,实际上做了”, dress up“着装”</strong></font>

   **"As it turned out to" 是一个词组，意为“事实证明”、“结果是”。这个词组通常用来引出一个意外或出乎意料的结局或结果，强调事实和现实。As it turned out, the train was delayed and I missed my flight. （结果火车晚点了，我错过了我的航班。）**

5. Ten students as well as the truck driver<u><font color=red><strong>      were hurt       </strong></font></u> in the accident and they were sent to hospital shortly after the accident. (hurt)

   十个学生以及卡车司机在事故中**严重受伤**，事后他们被立即送往了医院。

   <font color=red><strong>were hurt</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>主语后带有as well as短语时,谓语动词仍由主语决定,故此处谓语动词用复数形式, ten students 与hurt之间是被动关系,故用被动语态。</strong></font>

6. Perhaps the most important thing if we want to make a difference is <u><font color=red><strong>     to find what we like      </strong></font></u>to do. (find)

   如果我们想有所作为，也许最重要的就是**找到我们喜欢**做的事。

   <font color=red><strong>to find what we like</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>定式作表语表示主语的性质或职责等,what引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语；最后的“to do”是作目的状语，表明“找到我们喜欢做的事情”是为了实现“想要有所改变”的目的。</strong></font>

7. 一It's said that he was injured.

   一That's terrible. But with a little more care he <u><font color=red><strong>      could have avoided     </strong></font></u> this traffic accident. (avoid)

   一一据说他受伤了。

   一一太可怕了。但是如果仔细一点，他**本可以避免**这次交通事故的。

   <font color=red><strong>would/could have avoided</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>but后是与过去事实相反的假设,故句子谓语动词用 would/could have done的形式。</strong></font>

8. Festivals and celebrations of all kinds <u><font color=red><strong>     have been held      </strong></font></u> everywhere since ancient times. (hold)

   自古以来,世界各地就**举行**各种各样的节日和庆典。

   <font color=red><strong>have been held</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>and 连接并列成分作主语,不表示同一概念,故谓语动词用复数形式,主语与hold之间是被动关系,故用被动语态,且根据时间状语since ancient times可知用现在完成时.</strong></font>

9. The new bridge is <u><font color=red><strong>     three times the width of    </strong></font></u> that one built last year.(width)

   这座新桥比去年建的那座桥**宽三倍**。

   <font color=red><strong>three times the width of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>“倍数十width+ of...”表示“宽是……的多少倍”。"built"在这个句子中作为过去分词，用作形容词，修饰先行词"one"，表示“建造好的”。</strong></font>

10. Yichang <u><font color=red><strong>    is familiar to     </strong></font></u> many foreigners for the Three Georges. (familiar)

    宜昌因为三峡而为许多外国人**所熟悉**。

    <font color=red><strong>is familiar to</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>be familiar to“为……所熟悉”。</strong></font>
    
    



## lesson 35

1. He was getting more and more annoyed. Of course, <u><font color=red><strong>    the more upset      </strong></font></u>he was, the less he was able to concentrate. (upset)

   他越来越恼火。当然，他**越心烦**，就越不能集中注意力

   <font color=red><strong>the more upset</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>“the＋比较级,the十比较级”表示“越·…就越……”。</strong></font>

2. It was the first time in fifteen years<u><font color=red><strong>         that we had met         </strong></font></u>.(meet)

   那是十五年后**我们**的第一次**见面**。

   <font color=red><strong>that we had met</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>在句型“It was the first/second.. . time that...”句型中,用过去完成时态。</strong></font>

3. The book <u><font color=red><strong>     designed for      </strong></font></u>the children is very popular. (design)

   这本书是**专为**儿童**设计**的，它很受欢迎。

   <font color=red><strong>(which/that is) designed for</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>定语从句的先行词是 the book,引导词在从句中作主语,故用 which 或that,be designed for“为……设计”; the book 与design之间是被动关系,也可用动词-ed形式作定语。</strong></font>

4. John's success has nothing to do with good luck. It is years of hard work<u><font color=red><strong>       that has made him        </strong></font></u>what he is today. (make)

   约翰的成功与好运气无关。是多年的努力**使他成为**今天这样的。

   <font color=red><strong>that has made him</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句It is...that.. . ;make sb sth“使某人成为……”。</strong></font>

   **“have nothing to do with”是一个常用的短语，表示某事物或某人与另一件事物或另一个人没有关系或没有联系。例如：I have nothing to do with the company's decision.（我和公司的决定没有关系。）**

5. QQ has over 500 million members, which is almost<u><font color=red><strong>        twice the population of     </strong></font></u>the United States. ( population)

   QQ有着五亿的会员,这几乎是美国**人口的两倍**。

   <font color=red><strong>twice/two times the population of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>“倍数十the population of...”表示“人口是……的多少倍”。</strong></font>

6. Mr White<u><font color=red><strong>     should have arrived      </strong></font></u>at 8:30 for the meeting but he didn't turn up. (arrive)

   怀特先生**本应该到达**八点半的会议,但是他没有出现。

   <font color=red><strong>should have arrived</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>should have done“本应该做某事,实际上没做”。</strong></font>

7. Much attention<u><font color=red><strong>     should be paid to protecting       </strong></font></u>the rare animals and plants from dying out. (protect)

   **应该**多注意**保护**那些珍稀动植物以免灭绝。

   <font color=red><strong>should be paid to protecting</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>pay attention to doing sth.“关注做某事”,此处为被动形式。</strong></font>

   **"protect from"是一个常见的词组，表示保护某人或某物免受某种威胁或危险。通常使用该词组的结构是"protect someone/something from something"，其中的"something"表示具体的威胁或危险。例如：**

   - **Wearing sunscreen can protect your skin from the harmful effects of UV rays. （涂抹防晒霜可以保护皮肤免受紫外线的有害影响。）**
   - **The company installed a firewall to protect its computer system from hackers. （公司安装了防火墙，以保护其计算机系统免受黑客攻击。）**
   - **Parents should protect their children from exposure to violent or inappropriate content on the Internet. （父母应该保护孩子免受在互联网上接触暴力或不合适的内容的影响。）**

8. Only after they had performed hundreds of experiments<u><font color=red><strong>     did they solve     </strong></font></u>the problem. (solve)

   在做了几百次实验后，**他们才解决**那个问题。

   <font color=red><strong>did they solve</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>only修饰的状语置于句首时,主句用部分倒装,句中为一般过去时。</strong></font>

   **"hundreds of"是一个数量词短语，表示“数百个”或“许多”。通常用于描述数量比较多的人、事物或物品。例如：**

   - **There were hundreds of people waiting in line for the concert tickets. （有数百人在排队等待音乐会门票。）**
   - **The factory produces hundreds of cars every day. （这家工厂每天生产数百辆汽车。）**
   - **The museum has hundreds of paintings by famous artists. （这个博物馆有数百幅著名艺术家的画作。）**

   **需要注意的是，“hundreds of”后面通常跟可数名词的复数形式。**

9. There is no doubt<u><font color=red><strong>       that he will recover from       </strong></font></u> his injury in time for the race next week. ( recover)

   毫无疑问，**他会**及时**恢复**伤痛以参加下星期的比赛。

   <font color=red><strong>that he will recover from</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>doubt用在否定句中其后的引导词用that引导;recover from“从……中恢复过来”。</strong></font>

   - **"recover from"是一个短语，表示从某种疾病、伤害、精神压力等恢复过来。例如，“他需要一些时间来从手术中恢复过来”，可以翻译为“he needs some time to recover from the surgery”。**
   - **"There is no doubt" 是一个英语表达，意思是“毫无疑问”，“毫无争议”。这个短语通常用于强调某件事或观点的确切性或确定性，表示对事实或观点的肯定和信任。例如，“There is no doubt that he is the best candidate for the job.”（毫无疑问，他是这份工作的最佳人选。）**

10. He told me he<u><font color=red><strong>     determined to         </strong></font></u>work up the feelings of his audience. (determine)

    他告诉我他**决定**激发起听众的情感。

    <font color=red><strong>determined to</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>determine to do sth.“决定做某事”。</strong></font>





# part 06

## lesson 36

1. China together with some Asian countries <u><font color=red><strong>    was swept (up)      </strong></font></u> by Typhoon Haiyan on November 8th，causing great damage and deaths.(sweep)

   台风“海燕”11月8日**横扫了**中国和其他一些亚洲国家造成了巨大的损害和伤亡。

   <font color=red><strong>was swept (up)</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
