   <font color=red><strong>sweep/sweep up“横扫”；主语后带有together短语时，谓语动词与主语保持一致，此处用单数形式,China与sweep/sweep up之间是被动关系，且发生在过去，故用一般过去时的被动语态。</strong></font>

2. In a P. E. class, he nearly fell to the ground But fortunately, the teacher <u><font color=red><strong>    caught him by the arm     </strong></font></u> .(catch)

   在一节体育课上，他差点跌倒在地上。但幸运的是老师**抓住了他的胳膊**。

   <font color=red><strong>caught him by the arm</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>catch sb by the arm“抓住某人的胳膊”。</strong></font>

3. All the people concerned are wondering <u><font color=red><strong>    who it was      </strong></font></u> that let out the details of the draft plan.(who)

   所有有关的人都想知道**究竟是谁**泄露了计划草案的细节。

   <font color=red><strong>who it was</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句的特殊疑问句结构“疑问词十is it+that. ..”,宾语从句中要用陈述语序,且句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>

   **let out ：出租（房屋、土地等）;放出，释放（水、空气等）;呼（气）;发出（声音）**

4. With <u><font color=red><strong>      many universities to choose       </strong></font></u>，some students feel at loss when filling out college application. ( choose)

   在填报大学入学志愿时，由于**有许多大学可供选择**，很多学生感觉不知所措。

   <font color=red><strong>many colleges/universities to choose  </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>many colleges/universities 与choose 之间是被动关系,且表示将来意义，故用不定式的主动形式表示被动意义。</strong></font>

   **"With many universities to choose"是一个以介词短语"With"开头的独立分词结构，其中，分词短语"to choose"作定语修饰"universities"。整个结构的意思是"有很多大学可以选择"。**

5. When <u><font color=red><strong>   informed of         </strong></font></u>the news that many people were killed for an oil pipeline explosion in Qingdao,all of us felt shocked and deeply saddened. (inform)

   当**被告知**在青岛石油管道爆炸事件中有许多人丧生，我们都感到震惊和心痛。

   <font color=red><strong>informed of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>(we were) informed or/about主从句主语一致，we与inform之间是被动关系，故用被动语态；当主从句主语一致且含有be动词时，可以省略“主语十be”的形式。</strong></font>

   - **"Many"指的是“许多”的意思，它后面通常接可数名词的复数形式或不可数名词。例如，“Many people are afraid of spiders”（许多人害怕蜘蛛），“Many watermelons were sold at the market”（市场上卖出了许多西瓜）。**

   - **“Many of”是“许多...中的”的意思，后面要接可数名词的复数形式或不可数名词。例如，“Many of the students in this class are from different countries”（这个班级的许多学生来自不同的国家），“Many of the milk in the fridge has gone bad”（冰箱里的许多牛奶已经变质了）。**

   - **"All of"和"All"都可以表示全部或整个的意思，但它们的使用上有些不同。**

     **"All of"通常用来修饰可数名词或不可数名词，表示全部或整个。例如：**

     - **All of the students in the class passed the exam.**
     - **I drank all of the milk in the fridge.**

     **而"All"通常用来修饰可数名词或不可数名词，表示全部或整个，但是在一些情况下也可以省略"of"，特别是在口语中。例如：**

     - **I ate all the cake. (也可以说"All of the cake")**
     - **He finished all his homework. (也可以说"All of his homework")**

     **总的来说，"all of"更正式，而"all"更口语化，但是在大部分情况下它们可以互换使用。**

6. To beautify our city, a large number of old houses along the street <u><font color=red><strong>      have been pulled down       </strong></font></u> up to the present.(pull)

   为了美化城市，到目前为止大量沿街房屋**已经被拆除**。

   <font color=red><strong>have been pulled down</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>a large number of 修饰的名词作主语时谓语动词用复数形式，由时间状语up to the present可知用现在完成时。</strong></font>

   **"a large number of" 是一个表示数量的短语，意思是“大量的”，用于修饰可数或不可数名词的复数形式。与“many”或“much”类似，但“a large number of”更加强调数量的多少。**

   **例如：**

   - **A large number of people attended the concert.**
   - **The company has hired a large number of new employees this year.**
   - **The drought has caused a large number of crops to fail.**

7. Despite his <u><font color=red><strong>      interest in        </strong></font></u> writing，he left Oxford High School without graduating. (interest)

   虽然他**对**写作**感兴趣**，但是他还没有毕业就离开了牛津高级中学。

   <font color=red><strong>interest in</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>interest"兴趣”,与介词in搭配。</strong></font>

8. Eating too much<u><font color=red><strong>   is likely to     </strong></font></u>give one's stomach trouble. (likely)

   人吃太多**可能会**使得胃出现问题。

   <font color=red><strong>is likely to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be likely to“可能”。</strong></font>

9. It is so nice to hear from her,<u><font color=red><strong>     believe it or not        </strong></font></u>,we last met more than thirty years ago. (believe)

   收到她的信真是太好了。**信不信由你**，我们最后一次见面是在30多年以前。

   <font color=red><strong>Believe it or not</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>believe it or not“信不信由你”。</strong></font>

10. So<u><font color=red><strong>    was he addicted in     </strong></font></u>playing computer games that he neglected his study and fell behind.(addicted)

    **他**如此**沉迷于**玩电脑游戏以至于荒废了学业并且成绩掉队。
    
    <font color=red><strong>was he addicted in</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>so修饰的形容词置于可首时,句子用部分倒装；be addicted to“沉迷于”,句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>





## lesson 37

1. We were updating the teaching facilities in our school, so every teacher <u><font color=red><strong>    has been provided with       </strong></font></u> a laptop since the beginning of this term. (provide)

   我们正在升级我们学校的教学设备，所以本学期开学后每位老师都**配备**台笔记本电脑。

   <font color=red><strong>has been provided with</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>provide sb with sth.“提供给某人某物”,此处是其被动语态，且由时间状语since the beginning of this term可知用现在完成时。</strong></font>

2. Something terrible<u><font color=red><strong>   must have happened       </strong></font></u>if Li Chang was not coming to eat in his restaurant as he always did. (happen)

   如果李昌不像往常那样到他饭店里吃饭,那**一定是发生了**什么严重的事情。

   <font color=red><strong>must have happened</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>根据句意,对过去情况的肯定推测用must have done的形式。</strong></font>

3. Summer vacation is coming and his three children are all looking forward to<u><font color=red><strong>    traveling together with him        </strong></font></u>.(travel)

   暑假来了,他的三个孩子都盼望着**和他一起去旅游**。

   <font color=red><strong>traveling together with him</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>look forward to中的 to是介词,其后接动词-ing形式或名词。</strong></font>

4. About 1,000 local youths, the majority<u><font color=red><strong>    of whom belong to       </strong></font></u>wuhan University and HUST, will come to attend the celebration. (belong)

   约一千本地青年将参加庆典，**其中**大多数人**来自**武汉大学和华中科技大学。

   <font color=red><strong>of whom belong to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句为“the majority of+关系代词”引导的定语从句,引导词在从句中作介词 of的宾语,指代youths,故用whom.</strong></font>

5. It is reported that he was knocked down by the motorcycle running<u><font color=red><strong>     at an astonishing speed       </strong></font></u>.(astonish)

   据报道，他被辆**以惊人的速度**行驶的摩托车撞倒了。

   <font color=red><strong>at an astonishing speed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“以……的速度”,用介词at;astonishing“惊人的”。</strong></font>

6. He appeared very calm after he knew the result of his illness<u><font color=red><strong>    as if nothing had happened   </strong></font></u>(happen)

   得知他自己的病情后他显得非常镇定，**好像什么也没有发生一样**。

   <font color=red><strong>as if/though nothing had happened</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此处为方式状语从句,as if/though“好像”。</strong></font>

7. <u><font color=red><strong>       What impresses me most        </strong></font></u>is that whenever he appears in front of others, he wears a sincere smile. (impress)

   **我印象最深的**是，每当出现在别人面前时他总是面带真诚的微笑。

   <font color=red><strong>What impresses me most</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>所填部分为主语从句,引导词在从句中作主语,根据句意用 what。</strong></font>

   1. "impress sb" 是一个常用的词组，表示"给某人留下印象"。

      例如："He impressed the judges with his incredible talent."（他以其惊人的才华给评委留下了深刻印象。）

   2. be impressed by/with: 对...印象深刻

      例句：I was really impressed by her presentation.

   3. make an impression on: 对...产生印象

      例句：The speaker made a strong impression on the audience.

8. The newly-built stadium for the World Cup is <u><font color=red><strong>   double the size of     </strong></font></u>the old one in the center of the city.(size)

   为世界杯新修建的体育场是市中心老体育场**大小的两倍**。

   <font color=red><strong>twice/double the size of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>twice/double the size of“是……大小的两倍”。</strong></font>

9. It is widely accepted that one is<u><font color=red><strong>   more likely to succeed     </strong></font></u>at things he has already known well. (likely)

   人们普遍认为:一个人在他已经很熟悉的方面**更有可能成功**。

   <font color=red><strong>more likely to succeed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be likely to do sth.“有可能做某事”,句意表示“更有可能”,用比较级more.</strong></font>

   **"be likely to" 是一个常用的词组，表示某种情况或事件有可能发生或很有可能实现。其中的 "likely" 意为"可能的"，而 "be" 则是其常用的动词形式。例如：**

   - **It's likely to rain tomorrow. (明天有可能下雨。)**
   - **She's likely to be late for the meeting. (她很有可能会迟到开会。)**
   - **The team is likely to win the game. (这个团队很有可能赢得比赛。)**

   **在句子中，"be likely to" 后面通常接动词原形，表示某个动作可能会发生。**

10. Only when the class was over ;<u><font color=red><strong>     was he able to         </strong></font></u>play football with his friends on the playground.(able)

    只有下了课**他才能**和朋友们一起在操场上踢足球。

    <font color=red><strong>was he able to</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>only修饰的状语置于句首时，主句用部分倒装, be able to do sth.“能够做某事”。</strong></font>





## lesson 38

1. The class remained very noisy although the bell had rung five minutes before.  The teacher was about to lose his temper<u><font color=red><strong>     <font color=red><strong>when they settled down </strong></font>        </strong></font></u>(settle)

   五分钟前铃就响了但那个班还是非常吵闹。老师正要发脾气**这时他们突然安静下来了**。

   <font color=red><strong>when they settled down </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>settle down“安静”; be about to do. .. when...“正要做某事时突然……”。</strong></font>

2. Do you know how much time and effort they devoted<u><font color=red><strong>      to completing        </strong></font></u>such a complicated project?（complete）

   你知道**完成**这项复杂的工程他们倾注了多少时间和精力吗?

   <font color=red><strong>to completing</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>devote.. . to...“倾注……到……”, to是介词,其后接名词或动词-ing形式。</strong></font>

3. A person with a severe mental health problem is<u><font color=red><strong>        four times more likely      </strong></font></u>to have no close friends than the average. (likely)

   有严重心理疾病的人找不到知心朋友的**可能性**是普通人的**四倍**。

   <font color=red><strong>four times more likely</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“……是……的几倍”用“倍数＋...+than...”,表示“可能”,用likely .</strong></font>

4. The TV entertainment program, the Voice of China, enjoys great popularity，with a large audience<u><font color=red><strong>      lost in      </strong></font></u>its live show. (lose)

   电视娱乐节目《中国好声音)很受欢迎，很多观众**沉浸在**它的现场表演之中。

   <font color=red><strong>lost in</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“沉浸在……中”用“be lost in...”。</strong></font>

   **这句话的with部分可以被解释为独立主格结构，其中"with a large audience lost in its live show"是一个介词短语，作为整个句子的附加说明，修饰前面的主句。**

   1. **in large part: 大部分**

      **The success of the project is due in large part to his hard work.(这个项目的成功在很大程度上要归功于他的辛勤工作。)**

   2. **a large number of: 大量的**

      **A large number of people attended the concert.（许多人参加了音乐会。）**

   3. **large amount/quantity: 大量的**

      **She has a large amount of work to do.**

   4. **Large company: 大公司**

   5. **"a large"可以与名词连用，表示数量较多或规模较大的某个事物。**

      **There was a large crowd at the concert last night. （昨晚音乐会上有很多人。）**

5. <u><font color=red><strong>     Being occupied         </strong></font></u>with work should not be the reason for "treating one's neighbors as strangers".(occupy)

   工作**繁忙**不应该成为“对面不相识”的借口。

   <font color=red><strong>Being occupied/To be occupied/ That one is occupied </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be occupied with“被……占用”,此处既可用动词-ing形式作主语也可用不定式作主语,还可用主语从句的形式。</strong></font>

   **这句话的主语是"Being occupied with work"，其中"Being"是现在分词作主语（“Being”是一个现在分词，作为句子的主语。它没有表达被动语态的意思，而是表达了一种状态。这个句子的意思是“忙于工作不应该成为“把邻居当陌生人对待”的理由。”），相当于"Occupation with work"。谓语是"should not be"，表示否定推测。不定式短语"to treat one's neighbors as strangers"作为直接宾语。"the reason for"作为介词短语引出原因。整个句子是一个复合句，主句是"Being occupied with work should not be the reason"，其中"reason"作主语，谓语是"should not be"，意为"不应该是"。从句是"treating one's neighbors as strangers"，作为原因说明。**

6. Not until a week later<u><font color=red><strong>   was the issue put forward     </strong></font></u>at the meeting. (put)

   直到一周后，**这个问题才**在会议上**被提出**。

   <font color=red><strong>was the problem/issue/ question put forward</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>not until置于句首时句子用部分倒装; put forward“提出”,此处是其被动语态;problem/issue/question“问题”</strong></font>

7. Lily likes basketball very much, while volleyball is the sport<u><font color=red><strong>     which  I am fond of    </strong></font></u>.(fond)

   莉莉非常喜欢篮球，而排球是**我喜欢的**运动。

   <font color=red><strong>(which/that)I am fond of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>which/that引导定语从句,并在从句中作宾语,可省略,先行词是sport; be fond of“喜欢,喜爱”。</strong></font>

8. A forest is usually found<u><font color=red><strong>      where heavy rainfall        </strong></font></u>is frequent. (rainfall)

   森林经常在**大雨**很频繁的**地方**。

   <font color=red><strong>where heavy rainfall</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句为地点状语从句,引导词在从句中作地点状语,故用where.</strong></font>

9. His parents died when he was a baby. Nobody knows who it was<u><font color=red><strong>     that brought him up         </strong></font></u>.(bring)

   他是婴儿的时候父母就双亡了。没人知道究竟是谁**把他抚养成人的**。

   <font color=red><strong>that brought him up</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句的特殊疑问句式“疑问词+was it + that. ..”,宾语从句中用陈述语序;bring up“抚养”</strong></font>

10. Because of Typhoon Fitow this October, some citizens in this coastal city would rather they<u><font color=red><strong>     moved to        </strong></font></u>the inland area some day. (move)

    因为今年十月的台风“菲特”,这个沿海城市的一些市民宁愿有一天**搬到**内陆地区。

    <font color=red><strong>moved to</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>would rather后的宾语从句中要用虚拟语气,谓语动词用一般过去时表示与将来事实相反。</strong></font>





## lesson 39

1. Some plants can take in carbon dioxide we breathe out and <u><font color=red><strong>     in return       </strong></font></u>give oxygen to us. (return)

   一些植物能吸收我们呼出的二氧化碳，并且**作为报答**释放氧气给我们。

   <font color=red><strong>in return</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>in return“作为报答”。</strong></font>

2. Peter's jacket looked just the same as Jack's, but it cost <u><font color=red><strong>   double as much as     </strong></font></u> his. (much)

   彼得的夹克看上去和杰克的一模一样,但价格却是他的**两倍多**。

   <font color=red><strong>twice/double as much as</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>倍数修饰原级比较结构时,其结构为“倍数十as＋形容词/副词的原级十as"。</strong></font>

3. Einstein liked Bose's paper so much that he <u><font color=red><strong>    set aside      </strong></font></u>his own work and translated it into German. (set)

   爱因斯坦特别喜欢博斯的论文以至于他**把**自已的工作**放在一边**而把论文翻译成德文。

   <font color=red><strong>set aside</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>set aside“把……放到一边”。</strong></font>

4. Don't tell him the good news until<u><font color=red><strong>     the match finishes     </strong></font></u>.Otherwise he will be too excited to concentrate on the match. (finish)

   等到**比赛结束**后再告诉他这个好消息。否则他会太激动而不能集中精力比赛的。

   <font color=red><strong>the match finishes</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>根据句意“比赛结束”是将来要发生的事情,until引导的时间状语从句中常用一般现在时表示将来意义。</strong></font>

5. In our city there are several big public parks <u><font color=red><strong>     where many people go     </strong></font></u>to enjoy the beautiful scene. (go)

   在我们城市里有几个大的公共公园，**许多人都去那里**欣赏美景。

   <font color=red><strong>where/to which many people/persons go</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>定语从句的先行词是表示地点的parks,引导词在从句中作地点状语,故用where,根据go to...的搭配还可用to which代替。</strong></font>

6. The fact that smoking is harmful to health is <u><font color=red><strong>     admitted by most smokers       </strong></font></u>.( admit)

   吸烟有害健康的事实是**大多数吸烟者承认的**。

   <font color=red><strong>what most smokers admit/admitted by most smokers</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>is后可以看成是 what引导的表语从句,也可以看成是被动结构。</strong></font>

7. To their surprise, they found that the lecture given by the famous professor <u><font color=red><strong>    was easy to understand     </strong></font></u>(understand)

   让他们吃凉的是，他们发现这位著名教授的讲座**容易理解**。

   <font color=red><strong>was easy to understand</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>句中时态为一般过去时;be easy to do sth.“做某事容易”。</strong></font>

8. If I <u><font color=red><strong>    had said sorry         </strong></font></u> to him yesterday, he wouldn't be angry now. (say)

   如果我昨天向他**道歉**的话，他现在就不会生气了。

   <font color=red><strong>had said sorry</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>if引导的条件句表示与过去事实相反的假设,故谓语动词用过去完成时;say sorry to sb.“向某人道歉”。</strong></font>

9. Never before <u><font color=red><strong>     have we seen        </strong></font></u> a girl who can swim as fast as Ye Shiwen. (see)

   以前**我们**从来没有**见过**一个游泳可以像叶诗文一样快的女孩。

   <font color=red><strong>have we seen</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>否定词never 置于句首时,句子用部分倒装,且根据句意用现在完成时。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>     What is reported        </strong></font></u>in the newspaper is that seventeen climbers have been killed in the avalanche.(report)

    这份报纸上**报道的**是在这次雪崩中17个登山者遇难了。

    <font color=red><strong>What is reported</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>主语从句中的引导词在从句中作主语,表示具体意义,用 what.</strong></font>





## lesson 40

1. However<u><font color=red><strong>     hard I tried        </strong></font></u>to clear up the misunderstanding between them, they still ended up arguing with each other. (try)

   不管我怎样**努力尝试**去消除他们之间的误会，他们最后还是以争吵告终。

   <font color=red><strong>hard I tried</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>however引导让步状语从句时,其后跟形容词或副词,此处表示“努力”用 hard。</strong></font>

   - **hard ：adj.坚固的;坚硬的;结实的;adv.努力地;费力地;艰难地;**

     **Her job is hard work, but the pay is good.** 

   - **hardly ：adv.几乎不;几乎没有;尤用于can或could之后，主要动词之前，强调做某事很难;刚刚;才**

     **I can hardly hear you over the noise of the traffic**
     
   - **badly ：adv.非常;差;拙劣地;不认真仔细;不成功地;**

     **Things have been going badly**
     
   - **end up doing：结束;最终成为;做完某事**

     **We would end up doing nothing at all with our lives. （我们一生将一事无成。）**

   - **end up with：〈非正〉以…结束**

     **The weakest students can end up with a negative score.** 

     **最差的学生可能会以负分收场。**

2. A meteor exploded over this area. So far about 1, 200 people are reported <u><font color=red><strong>       to have been injured       </strong></font></u>.(injure)
   一颗陨石在这个地区上空爆炸。到目前为止，据报已有大约1,200人**受伤**。

   <font color=red><strong>to have been injured</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be reported to do sth.“据报道…”，此处不定式表示的动作发生在be reported之后,且由时间状语可知用现在完成时。</strong></font>
   
   **So far：目前为止，迄今为止;（只能到）如此程度，这个地步**
   
3. Mary<u><font color=red><strong>    couldn't have referred to       </strong></font></u>the dictionary,  because she didn't give me an accurate explanation of the word.(refer)
   玛丽**一定没查过**词典，因为她没给我这个词的准确解释。

   <font color=red><strong>can't/couldn't have referred to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去情况的否定推测用can't/couldn't have done的形式，没有must not have done的形式。</strong></font>
   
   1. **refer to ：v.查阅;提到**
   2. **accurate ：adj.精确的;正确无误的;准确的**
   3. **exact ：adj.准确的;精确的;严谨的;严格的;**
   4. **explanation ：n.解释;说明;阐述;解释性说法;说明性文字**
   
4. It was completely wrong that not until the accident happened<u><font color=red><strong>    did people focus on     </strong></font></u>the problem. (focus)
   直到事故发生之后**人们才关注**这个问题这是完全错误的。

   <font color=red><strong>did people focus on</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>not until置于句首时句子用部分倒装，句中时态为一般过去时; focus on“关注”。</strong></font>
   
   **"Not until" 和 "not...until" 的区别在于语法结构和语义上的差异。**
   
   - **"Not until" 是一个连词短语，用来表示某个动作直到某个时间才发生。其基本结构为 "not until + 时间状语从句"，表示 "直到……才" 的意思。**
   
     **例如：Not until she finished her homework did she go to bed.（直到她完成作业才去睡觉。）**
   
   - **"Not...until" 是一个复合连词，也用来表示某个动作直到某个时间才发生。其基本结构为 "not + 动词/情态动词 + until + 时间状语"，表示 "直到……才" 的意思。**
   
     **例如：I won't leave until he comes back.（他回来之前我不会离开。）**
   
   **总体来说，"not until" 的语义更为强烈，强调了某个动作在之前一直未发生，而 "not...until" 则相对中性一些，只是简单地表达了时间关系**
   
5. <u><font color=red><strong>      It remains to be seen       </strong></font></u>whether a favorite play among Chinese viewers,Legend of Zhen Huan, will be accepted by foreign audience. (remain)

     备受中国观众喜爱的电视剧《甄嬡传》能否被外国观众接受还**有待观察**。

     <font color=red><strong>It remains to be seen</strong></font>

     <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

     <font color=red><strong>remains to be done“有待被做”,此句中主语后置,用it作形式主语。</strong></font>

     **"It remains to be done"是一个常用的句型，意思是"还有待完成"或"尚未完成"，通常用于强调某件事情还没有做完或还有需要做的事情。**

     1. **We have finished writing the report, but the editing and proofreading remain to be done.**

        **我们已经完成了报告的写作，但编辑和校对还有待完成。**

     2. **The project is not yet complete; there are several tasks that remain to be done.**

        **项目还没有完成，还有几项任务有待完成。**

     3. **The research has been successful, but further investigation remains to be done.**

        **研究已经取得了成功，但还有进一步的调查工作需要完成。**

6. Had it not been for the worsening air quality, the flight<u><font color=red><strong>      wouldn't have been delayed     </strong></font></u>by the heavy fog for such a long time. (delay)

   如果不是空气质量越来越差，航班**不会**因为大雾**延误**如此之久。

   <font color=red><strong>wouldn't have been delayed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>条件句表示与过去事实相反,主句谓语动词用 would have done的形式。</strong></font>

   **worsening ：v.(使)变得更坏，变得更糟，恶化 ;n.恶化；变坏;adj.日益恶化的**

7. It was only after serious consideration<u><font color=red><strong>       that he decided      </strong></font></u>to sponsor the poor child to finish his compulsory education. (decide)

   就是在慎重考虑后，**他才决定**资助这个贫困孩子完成义务教育的。

   <font color=red><strong>that he decided</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为强调句式It was...that...句式,句中时态为一般过去时。</strong></font>

   **compulsory ：adj.(因法律或规则而)必须做的，强制的，强迫的;义务的**

8. He used only half of the money,<u><font color=red><strong>     the rest of which was saved     </strong></font></u>for other purposes. (save)

   他仅用了一半的钱，**其余的节省下来**留作它用。

   <font color=red><strong>the rest of which was saved/and the rest of it was saved</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句可看成是“the rest of+关系代词”引导的非限制性定语从句,先行词表示物,引导词用which;还可看成是and连接的两个句子,第二个句子中用被动语态。</strong></font>

9. By the time her father retires, probably she<u><font color=red><strong>    will have taken over     </strong></font></u>the company. (take)

   到她父亲退休时，很可能她**已经接管了**公司。

   <font color=red><strong>will have taken over</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>take over“接管”,时间状语by the time her father retires表示将来意义,故此处用将来完成时。</strong></font>

10. <u><font color=red><strong>      Having been warned of      </strong></font></u>the possible snowstorm at hand, they determined to stay at home for the holiday.(warn)

     **得到告诫**可能有暴风雪即将到来,他们决定假期待在家里。

     <font color=red><strong>Having been warned of/Warned of/After they were/have been warned of</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>逻辑主语they与 warn之间是被动关系,故用动词-ed形式作状语,根据句意可用现在完成时也可用一般过去时;还可以将此处看成是 after连接的句子,句中可用一般过去时也可用现在完成时。</strong></font>
    
    1. **"Be warned of"是一个表示警告或提醒的短语，意思是"注意，警惕"，常用于提醒某人注意某种情况或可能出现的问题。**
       - **Be warned of the strong currents in the river before you go swimming. （在你去游泳前要注意这条河流的强水流。）**
       - **I was warned of the potential dangers of the new medication by my doctor.（我的医生提醒我这种新药可能存在的潜在风险。）**
    2. **at hand 手头;在手边，在附近，即将来临**
    3. **possible ：adj.可能的;可能;能做到(或取得);**
    4. **以下是表示计划、安排、打算的一些常见动词和词组：**
       1. **plan：计划，常用于表示长期、具体、有条理的计划，例如：**
          - **We are planning to expand our business into Asia next year.**
          - **I have planned my schedule for the whole week.**
       2. **arrange：安排，强调根据具体情况做出的安排和调整，例如：**
          - **I need to arrange a meeting with my supervisor next week.**
          - **We have arranged to meet at the airport at 8 am.**
       3. **schedule：安排时间表，指按照时间顺序列出一系列活动的安排，例如：**
          - **The conference schedule has been finalized and sent to all attendees.**
          - **I need to schedule a doctor's appointment for next week.**
       4. **intend：打算，指有意愿去做某事，例如：**
          - **I intend to take a break from work and travel next month.**
          - **She intends to study abroad after she finishes her degree.**
       5. **aim：计划，指为达到某一目的而制定的计划，例如：**
          - **The company aims to increase its sales by 20% next year.**
          - **My aim is to finish the project by the end of this month.**
       6. **propose：提议，指向别人提出计划或建议，例如：**
          - **He proposed a new marketing strategy to the team.**
          - **She proposed that we have a team-building activity next month.**





## lesson 41

1. He firmly argued that at no time<u><font color=red><strong>      did they regard examinations     </strong></font></u>as the only means of stimulating pupils to pursue knowledge. (regard)

   他坚定地表明**他们**从来没有**把考试**看成是激励学生学习知识的唯一手段。

   <font color=red><strong>did they regard/had they regarded examinations/exams</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>at no time置于句首时句子用部分倒装,句中可用一般过去时也可用过去完成时;exam,examination要用复数形式。</strong></font>

   - **argue ：v.争论;争吵;争辩;论证;说理;证明;表明**
   - **stimulating ：adj.趣味盎然的;激励人的;振奋人心的; v.促进;激发;激励;刺激;使兴奋**
   - **stimulate ：vt.促进;激发;激励;刺激;使兴奋;促进(身体某部分)的功能**
   - **pupils ：学生;(尤指)小学生**
   - **pursue ：v.追求;致力于;执行;**

2. Far from<u><font color=red><strong>      being a modest person       </strong></font></u>，she would make use of every possible chance to show off what she had achieved. (modest)

   她不是**一个谦逊的人**，她总是利用每一个可能的机会炫耀自己取得的成绩。

   <font color=red><strong>being modest/being a modest person</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>根据提示及 far from的用法,此处用动词-ing形式作介词的宾语。</strong></font>

   1. **Far from" 是一个英语短语，表示某事与某种期望或预期的情况完全相反，常用于修饰形容词或副词。**

      1. **Far from being happy, he was miserable.（他并不快乐，相反很痛苦。）**
      2. **Far from improving, the situation has actually gotten worse.（情况并没有改善，相反却更加糟糕了。）**
      3. **Far from arriving on time, he was more than an hour late.（他远远没有按时到达，相反晚了一个多小时。）**

      **在这些例子中，"far from" 表示事实与期望完全相反，强调情况的不同于预期的情况。**

3. Tom knew that anybody who stole his phone<u><font color=red><strong>        wouldn't be so foolish       </strong></font></u>as to use it right in front of him.(foolish)

   汤姆知道不管是谁偷了他的手机都**不会愚蠢到**在他的面前使用它。

   <font color=red><strong>wouldn't/couldn't be so foolish</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>句中时态为一般过去时,表示“不会,不可能”用 wouldn't 或couldn't; be foolish to do sth.“做某事愚蠢”。</strong></font>

   **英语中有so...as...句型，用于比较两个事物的相似程度。这个句型通常用于肯定句，表达“像……一样”的意思。其结构为：so + 形容词/副词原级 + as + 名词短语/从句。**

   - **She is so beautiful as to be mistaken for a movie star.（她非常漂亮，以至于被误认为是电影明星。）**
   - **He runs so fast as to break the world record.（他跑得如此快，以至于打破了世界纪录。）**

4. No matter what he says now I do believe that he as well as I<u><font color=red><strong>      is responsible for       </strong></font></u>it. (responsible)

   不管他现在说什么,我坚持认为他和我一样对这件事是**有责任的**。

   <font color=red><strong>is responsible for</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be responsible for“为……负责”;主语后带有as well as短语时,谓语动词由主语决定,故此处用is.</strong></font>

5. <u><font color=red><strong>       In a word          </strong></font></u>，she didn't like living in London at all, (word)

   **总而言之**，她根本就不喜欢在伦敦生活。

   <font color=red><strong>In a word</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>in a word“总而言之”。</strong></font>

6. The city has become<u><font color=red><strong>    more and more beautiful       </strong></font></u>thanks to the environment improvement program. (beautiful)

   多亏了这一改善环境的工程,这个城市变得**越来越美丽**了。

   <font color=red><strong>more and more beautiful</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>“比较级＋比较级”表示“越来越”，beautiful的比较级是借助more.</strong></font>

   **improvement ：n.改善;改进;改进处;改善的事物**

7. <u><font color=red><strong>        The instant I went upstairs      </strong></font></u>into the master bedroom I told Hilary we had to buy the house., (instant)

   **我一上楼走进**主卧室,我就告诉希拉里说,"这房子我们买定了"

   <font color=red><strong>The instant I walked/went upstairs</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>the instant“一……一就……引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>

   **master n.(男)主人，雇主;主宰;有控制力的人;**

8. Computers have been used widely to keep<u><font color=red><strong>       the traffic running          </strong></font></u>smoothly. (run)

   计算机被广泛地应用以使**交通运行**得顺畅。

   <font color=red><strong>the traffic running</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>keep sth doing“使某物做某事”,动词-ing形式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

   **smoothly ：adv.平稳地;顺利地;连续而流畅地;平静地;自信地;平整地**

   **smooth ：adj.平整的;平坦的;平滑的;光滑的 ；vt.使平整;使平坦;使平滑;**

9. If<u><font color=red><strong>     I had known       </strong></font></u>I would meet such a big trouble, I might not live here now.(know)

   如果**我知道**我会遇到这么大的麻烦，我可能现在就不会住在这里了。

   <font color=red><strong>I had known</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>if条件句表示与过去事实相反的假设,谓语动词用过去完成时。</strong></font>

10. The last time we had great fun was<u><font color=red><strong>     when we were visiting       </strong></font></u>the Water Park. (visit)

    我们最后一次玩得高兴是**我们正参观**水上乐园**的时候**。
    
    <font color=red><strong>when we were visiting</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>表语从句的引导词在从句中作时间状语,故用when.</strong></font>





## lesson 42

1. But for his help, we<u><font color=red><strong>     couldn't have finished      </strong></font></u>the program in time. (finish)

   要是没有他的帮忙，我们就**不可能**按时**完成**这个项目了。

   <font color=red><strong>couldn't have finished </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>but for表示的条件与过去事实相反,根据句意主句谓语动词用couldn't have done的形式。</strong></font>

2. With<u><font color=red><strong>   many problems arising    </strong></font></u>， he didn't know what to do next. (arise)

   随着**很多问题的出现**，他不知道下一步该做什么了。

   <font color=red><strong>many problems arising</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此句为 with的复合结构,逻辑主语many problems与 arise之间是主动关系,故用“with＋名词＋动词-ing形式”。</strong></font>

   1. **lie & lay**

      - **lie ：put your body in a horizontal position（将你的身体放在水平位置）；躺;平躺;平卧;平放;**

        **第三人称单数：lies；复数：lies ；现在分词：lying；过去式：lay lied；过去分词：lain lied**

        <font color=red><strong>I need to lie down for a few minutes.</strong></font>

      - **lay:  put something or somebody in a horizontal position（使某物或某人处于水平位置）；放置;(尤指轻轻地或小心地)安放;铺放;**

        **第三人称单数：lays；现在分词：laying；过去式：laid；过去分词： laid**

        <font color=red><strong>Lay the textbook flat on the desk</strong></font>

   2. **raise & rise & arise** 

      - **raise ：go up**

        **第三人称单数： raises； 现在分词： raising；  过去式： raised；  过去分词： raised**

        <font color=red><strong>She raised the gun and fired.</strong></font>

      - **rise ：make something go up**

        **第三人称单数：rises；现在分词：rising；过去式：rose；过去分词：risen**

        <font color=red><strong> It's hard not to rise your voice when you're arguing with someone.</strong></font>

      - **arise ：to happen; to start to exist 发生;出现;(由…)引起;(因…)产生;**

        **第三人称单数：arises；现在分词： arising；过去式： arose；过去分词： arisen**

        <font color=red><strong>A storm arose during the night.</strong></font>

3. <u><font color=red><strong>       It won't be long           </strong></font></u>before we take the college entrance examination, (long)

   **要不了多久**我们就要参加高考了。

   <font color=red><strong>It won't be long </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it won't be long before. ..“不久就·……”。</strong></font>

   1. **It will be + 一段时间 + before...**

      <font color=red>**“It will be + 一段时间 + before...”这个句式用来表达某个事情要经过一段时间才会发生或实现，通常表示等待、耐心等待或延迟。这个句式中的“before”表示在某个时间之前，而“it”则用来代替具体的主语，通常指前文提到的某个事情或情况。**</font>

      - **It will be months before we finish the construction of the new building.（新建筑物的建设需要数月时间。）**

      <font color=red>**需要注意的是，这个句式通常用于表达一种乐观的期望，而不是对事情的消极态度。**</font>

   2. **It won't be+一段时间+before...**

      <font color=red>**"It won't be + 一段时间 + before"是一个否定句式，表示某事不会在一段时间内发生或完成。**</font>

      - **It won't be long before we finish this project.（我们很快就会完成这个项目。）**
      - **It won't be until next week before we can start the training.（我们要等到下周才能开始培训。）**

      <font color=red>**这个句式常用于表示等待或延迟的情况，通常和一个时间短语一起使用，用来说明要等多久才能实现某个目标或完成某个任务。在句子中，时间短语通常放在句首或句尾。需要注意的是，这个句式中的时间短语可以是任意一种时间单位，如“a week”，“a month”，“a year”等。**</font>

   3. **entrance** 

      **n.入口(处);进入;大门(口);通道;出场;**

      **vt.使狂喜;使入迷**

4. He<u><font color=red><strong>        pretended to be reading      </strong></font></u>aloud in the study when he heard his father open the door. (pretend)

   当他听到爸爸的开门声，他**假装**在书房大声**读书**。

   <font color=red><strong>pretended to be reading</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>句中时态为一般过去时,pretend to do“假装在做某事”,由句意可知“正在读书”,用过去进行时。</strong></font>

   1. **aloud adv.出声地;大声地**

   2. **loud adj.大声的;响亮的;喧闹的;俗艳的;花哨的；adv.大声地;喧闹地;响亮地**

   3. **quietly adv.安静地;平静地;在暗中;轻声地;秘密地;温和地**

   4. **quiet adj.轻声的;安静的;平静的;克制的；n.宁静;寂静;平静;安静；v.(使)平静，安静**

   5. **alone adj./adv.单独地;单独;独自;孤独;**

   6. **lonely adj.孤独的;寂寞的;在孤单中度过的**

      **Although he lives alone, he doesn't feel lonely**

5. Having spent some time in the city, he had no trouble<u><font color=red><strong>    in finding the way to    </strong></font></u>the History Museum. (find)

   他在这个城市已经待了一段时间，因此毫不费力就**找到了去**历史博物馆**的路**。

   <font color=red><strong>(in）finding the road/way to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>分词短语 "Having spent some time in the city" 是以现在分词的形式出现的，表示一个已经完成且是主动的动作。have no trouble in doing sth.“做某事没有困难”,类似have difficulty in doing sth， in可以省略。</strong></font>

6. So<u><font color=red><strong>     occupied have I been       </strong></font></u>with my work that I haven't had time for social activities. (occupy)

   **我一直忙于**工作，以至于没有时间去参加社交活动。

   <font color=red><strong>occupied have I been</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>so修饰的状语置于句首时,句子用部分倒装,根据句意用现在完成时,be occupied with“被……占用”</strong></font>

   1. **social adj.社会的;社会上的;社会地位的；n.联谊会;联欢会**
   2. **society n.社会(共同遵守一定的习俗、法律等的特定群体);学会;协会;社团;**
   3. **socially adv.社会上;交际上;和睦地**

7. When we went shopping last week, Mary spent<u><font color=red><strong>     half as much money        </strong></font></u>as I did. (much)

   我们上周去购物的时候，玛丽花掉的钱只有我花掉的**一半多**。

   <font color=red><strong>half as much money</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“……的一半”,用“half+as. . . as. ..”.</strong></font>

8. Now that Lucy is out of work, she<u><font color=red><strong>    has been considering going back        </strong></font></u>to school, but she hasn't decided yet. (consider)

   因为露西失业了，她**一直在考虑**回学校,但还没决定。

   <font color=red><strong>has been considering going back</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>根据句意可知“考虑回学校”是从过去某时开始一直持续到现在,且还可能继续持续下去的动作,用现在完成进行时。</strong></font>

   1. **now that 既然;由于**

   2. **consider doing sth 考虑做某事**

      **I'm considering moving to a new city for a change of scenery. （我正在考虑搬到一个新城市换个环境。）**

   3. **go back**

      **"go back" 是一个常用的英语短语，表示“返回”、“回到以前的位置或状态”之意。**

      **I need to go back to my office to get my laptop.（我需要回到办公室拿我的笔记本电脑。）**

9. Lily was badly hurt in an accident, and the only thing<u><font color=red><strong>    that she could do        </strong></font></u>was to lie in bed to recover.(do)

   莉莉在一场事故中严重受伤，**她**唯一**能做的**就是躺在床上等待康复。

   <font color=red><strong>(that) she could/can do</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>先行词被the only修饰时,引导词只能用that,此处that在从句中作宾语,可省略。</strong></font>

   - **incident日常小事;有预谋的政治事件**
   - **accident无法预料的事故或灾难**

10. Harry went to the bank because he<u><font color=red><strong>      was short of money      </strong></font></u>.(short)

    哈里去了银行，因为他**缺钱**了。

    <font color=red><strong>was short of money</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>be short of“缺……”,句中为一般过去时。</strong></font>

    1. **be short of**

       **"Be short of"通常用于指时间、金钱、资源等实物不足的情况，可以用于描述某人或某物需要的数量不足，**

       - **We're short of time.（我们时间不够了。）**
       - **The company is short of money.（公司资金不足。）**
       - **The team was short of players.（球队缺少球员。）**
    
    2. **be lack of**
    
       **"Be lack of"通常用于指缺乏抽象的事物，如能力、经验、素质等，通常用于描述人或事物本身的特征缺乏**
    
       - **He is lacking in confidence.（他缺乏自信。）**
       - **The report is lacking in detail.（报告缺乏细节。）**
       - **The team is lacking in experience.（球队缺乏经验。）**
    
       **需要注意的是，"be lack of"通常不用于描述实物数量的不足，而是强调事物本身的缺陷。**







# part 07

## lesson 43

1. My mother is excellent in her work as well as<u><font color=red><strong>        keeping everything in order         </strong></font></u>.(keep)

   我的母亲在工作上很出色，而且能**使一切都井井有条**。

   <font color=red><strong>keeping everything in order</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>as well as为介词短语,故其后用动词-ing形式;keep后可跟介词短语作宾语补足语, in order“井井有条”</strong></font>

   1. **is excellent in 表示某人或某物在某方面表现出色或突出，是一个常见的表达方式。其中，“excellent”意为“出色的，优秀的”，“in”表示某个领域或方面。**

      **This restaurant is excellent in service. （这家餐厅在服务方面很优秀。）**
      
   2. **as well as 以及，既…又…，除…之外（也），此外**

2. <u><font color=red><strong>      It was on this point         </strong></font></u>that I didn't agree with him. (point)

   **正是在这一点**上，我不同意他的意见。

   <font color=red><strong>It was on this point</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句中用到了强调句式“It+be十被强调部分十that...”,被强调部分为on this point;表示在某一点上应用介词on,由后半句中的时态可知此处用一般过去时。</strong></font>

   **"Agree" 是一个常用的动词，表示同意或赞同某种想法、观点、建议等。以下是一些常见的和 "agree" 相关的短语：**

   1. **agree with：与某人或某事物的观点、意见相同，或是同意某种做法。 例句：I agree with your opinion on this matter.（我同意你对这件事的看法。）**
   2. **agree to：同意或接受某种提议或建议。 例句：I have agreed to the terms of the contract.（我已经同意了合同的条款。）**
   3. **agree on/upon：就某个问题或某种事情达成共识或协议。 例句：The two parties finally agreed upon the terms of the settlement.（两方最终就和解条款达成了一致。）**
   4. **agree in principle：在原则上同意某种想法或提议，但细节还需要讨论和商定。 例句：We agree in principle to your proposal, but we need to work out the details.（我们在原则上同意你的建议，但需要讨论细节。）**
   5. **agree to disagree：同意不同意见，认为进一步争辩没有意义。 例句：We agreed to disagree on this matter and moved on to other topics.（我们同意各自的不同意见，转而讨论其他话题。）**
   6. **agree with someone/something on something：在某个问题或某种事情上与某人或某事物达成共识。 例句：I finally agreed with my boss on the new project plan.（我终于和老板在新项目计划上达成了共识。）**

   **需要注意的是， "agree" 后面可以跟不同的介词和副词，具体用法取决于句子的语境和所表达的意思。**

3. It is easy to see<u><font color=red><strong>       why her friends call        </strong></font></u>her the“smiling angel in a wheelchair“. (call)

   很容易可以看出**为什么她的朋友们称呼**她为“轮椅上的微笑天使”。

   <font color=red><strong>why her friends call</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>why引导宾语从句,并在从句中作原因状语。</strong></font>

4. The plants in our garden<u><font color=red><strong>    would have grown better         </strong></font></u>if it had not rained so much last year. (grow)

   去年如果没有下这么多雨的话，我们花园里的植物**可以长得更好**。

   <font color=red><strong><font color=red><strong>could/would/should/might have grown better</strong></font></strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由语境可知,此处是对过去情况的虚拟,此时主句谓语动词用could/would/should/might have done的形式。</strong></font>

   **grown：adj.成熟的;成年的;长大的 v.扩大;增加;增强;长大;长高;发育;成长;(使)生长grow的过去分词**

5. Like other Disney Parks, Hong Kong Disney Land<u><font color=red><strong>     is made up of        </strong></font></u>several“lands”，each offering different experiences. (make)

   像其他的迪士尼乐园样，香港迪土尼乐园**由**几个“园”**组成**，每一个都提供不同的体验。

   <font color=red><strong>is made up of</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>be made up of“由……组成”。</strong></font>

   **在定语从句中，“offering”是一个现在分词，用作“which/that are offering”这个从句的谓语，表示被修饰的“lands”正在“提供”不同的体验。现在分词常常被用来形成非限制性定语从句，用于修饰主句中的名词或代词，强调其重要性或者特定的特征。**

   **需要注意的是，由于现在分词的主动形式具有形容词的性质，因此它可以在句子中作为定语或者表语。在这个例句中，非限制性定语从句中的“offering”修饰“lands”，相当于“which/that are offering”，表示“正在提供”不同的体验。**

   make是一个非常常见的动词，有很多用法和短语。下面列举一些常见的用法和例子：

   1. **make friends with sb：和某人交朋友。例如：She quickly made friends with her new classmates.**
   2. **make a decision：做决定。例如：It's time for us to make a decision on this matter.**
   3. **make a difference：产生影响。例如：Every little bit helps and can make a difference.**
   4. **make a plan：制定计划。例如：Let's make a plan for our next vacation.**
   5. **make a mistake：犯错误。例如：I made a mistake on the math problem.**
   6. **make an effort：努力尝试。例如：He made an effort to learn a new skill.**
   7. **make progress：取得进展。例如：The company has made great progress in developing new products.**
   8. **make money：赚钱。例如：She started her own business to make money.**
   9. **make sense：有意义、合理。例如：What she said didn't make any sense to me.**
   10. **make sure：确保。例如：Can you make sure that the door is locked before we leave?**

   这些都是make的常见用法和短语，当然还有很多其他的用法和短语。

   1. **make up：组成；化妆；弥补**
      1. **The committee is made up of ten members.（委员会由十名成员组成。）**
      2. **She made up her face before going to the party.（她去聚会前化了妆。）**
      3. **He will have to work overtime to make up the lost time.（他将不得不加班赶时间。）**
   2. **make out：辨认出；理解；填写（表格等）**
      1. **I can't make out what you are saying.（我听不清你在说什么。）**
      2. **It was difficult to make out the meaning of the ancient text.（很难辨认出古代文本的含义。）**
      3. **Could you help me make out this form?（你能帮我填写这张表格吗？）**
   3. **make for：前往；促成**
      1. **They made for the nearest exit.（他们朝最近的出口走去。）**
      2. **This policy will make for greater economic stability.（这项政策将促进更大的经济稳定。）**
   4. **make into：制成；变成**
      1. **She made the clay into a vase.（她把黏土制成了一个花瓶。）**
      2. **He hopes to make his hobby into a career.（他希望把自己的兴趣变成一份职业。）**
   5. **make of：理解；认为**
      1. **I don't know what to make of this situation.（我不知道该如何理解这种情况。）**
      2. **What do you make of his proposal?（你认为他的提议怎么样？）**
   6. **make over：改造；移交**
      1. **The old building was made over into a modern office.（那栋老建筑被改造成了现代化的办公室。）**
      2. **She made over the ownership of the company to her son.（她把公司的所有权移交给了她的儿子。）**
   7. **make through：完成；度过**
      1. **We finally made through the project after many sleepless nights.（我们经过多个不眠之夜，终于完成了这个项目。）**
      2. **I don't know how we're going to make through this difficult time.（我不知道我们该如何度过这个艰难的时期。）**
   8. **make up for：弥补；补偿**
      1. **He tried to make up for his mistake by working harder.（他试图通过更努力地工作来弥补自己的错误。）**
      2. **She brought a gift to make up for missing the party.（她带了一份礼物以弥补缺席聚会的过失。）**

6. <u><font color=red><strong>      In case I forget     </strong></font></u>， please remind me of my bike which is still under repair. (case)

   **万一我忘记**，请提醒我我的自行车还在修理中。

   <font color=red><strong>In case I forget</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>in case“以防万一”,引导条件状语从句。</strong></font>

   - **in my case ：就我来说**

     **In my case I chose that course which I considered right （至于我呢，就选择了我认为正确的那条路线。）**

   - **in my opinion ：我的意见是**

     **In my opinion, I think it is a wonderful country. （我的意见是，这是一个美妙的国度。）**
     
   - **in which case 在那种情况下;那样的话;在那种情况下**

7. Shirley<u><font color=red><strong>     was writing           </strong></font></u>a book about China last year, but I don't know whether she has finished it. (write)

   雪莉去年**在写**一本关于中国的书，但是我不知道她是否已经完成了。

   <font color=red><strong>was writing</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示过去某段时间一直在做的事情用过去进行时。</strong></font>

8. Sydney is the biggest city in Australia, which has many places of interest,<u><font color=red><strong>      among which is      </strong></font></u>the Opera House. (which)

   悉尼是澳大利亚最大的城市,那里有很多名胜古迹,**其中就有**歌剧院。

   <font color=red><strong>among which is</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此处为“介词十关系代词”引导定语从句,由“其中”可知,介词用among.</strong></font>

   - **places of interest ：名胜古迹**

   - **interest** 

     **n.兴趣;关注;引人关注的性质;吸引力;趣味;业余爱好;利益;利息;好处;（企业或公司的）股份;利害关系;同行**
     **vt.使感兴趣;使关注**

   - **介词+关系代词通常用来引导定语从句，这种结构通常出现在主句的名词或代词后面，用来修饰或说明这个名词或代词。**

     1. **in which: 在其中**
        **例句：This is the museum in which the ancient artifacts are displayed.(这是展示古代文物的博物馆。)**
     2. **of which: 其中的**
        **例句：The house, of which the roof was damaged, needed repairs.(这所屋顶受损的房子需要修理。)**
     3. **for which: 为了哪个**
        **例句：He has bought a new camera for which he paid a lot of money.(他花了很多钱买了一台新相机。)**
     4. **on which: 在哪个上面**
        **例句：The painting, on which he spent many hours, was finally finished.(他花了好几个小时画的这幅画终于完成了。)**
     5. **by which: 通过哪个**
        **例句：This is the method by which we can solve the problem.(这就是我们解决这个问题的方法。)**
     6. **with which: 用哪个**
        **例句：She wrote the letter with the pen with which I had just signed the contract.(她用我刚刚签署合同的钢笔写了这封信。)**
     7. **at which: 在哪个地方**
        **例句：The party will be held at the restaurant at which we had dinner last time.(聚会将在我们上次吃晚饭的餐厅举行。)**
     8. **to which: 到哪个**
        **例句：This is the address to which the letter should be sent.(这是信件应该寄到的地址。)**

   - **在正式的英语书面语中，应该用“for whom”引导定语从句，而不是“for who”。因为“whom”是关系代词，代表宾格，而在定语从句中，关系代词所在的位置相当于一个宾语，应该使用宾格形式。虽然在口语或非正式场合中，人们有时可能会使用“for who”，但这在正式的英语书面语中是不被认可的。**

     **举个例子：**

     - **The scholarship is intended for students for whom English is not their first language.（正确）**

       **该奖学金是为英语不是第一语言的学生准备的**

     - **The scholarship is intended for students for who English is not their first language.（不正确）**

9. He<u><font color=red><strong>       must have completed          </strong></font></u>his work; otherwise he wouldn't be enjoying himself by the seaside.(complete)

   他**肯定完成了**工作,否则他不会在海边玩得这么痛快。

   <font color=red><strong>must have completed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去情况的肯定推测用 must have done的形式。</strong></font>

   - **"by" 在 "by the seaside" 中作为介词使用。它表示位置，意思是“在……旁边，在……附近”。 "By the seaside" 的意思是“在海边”。**

   - **"Be enjoying oneself"是一个表示正在愉悦地度过时间的短语，通常用来描述某个人在某个活动或场合中感到非常愉快和放松**

     **She is really enjoying herself at the party, chatting with friends and dancing to the music.（她在聚会上玩得很开心，和朋友聊天，跟着音乐跳舞。）**

     **这个短语中的"oneself"是反身代词，表示主语是自己。所以，这个短语通常用于第三人称单数和复数形式。**

10. Two tennis courts as well as a swimming pool<u><font color=red><strong>     are available for        </strong></font></u>the regular members of the club.(available)

    有两个网球场和一个游泳池**供**俱乐部的固定会员**使用**。
    
    <font color=red><strong>are available for</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>as well as连接两个名词时,谓语动词的形式由主语决定,故此处用复数形式; be available for“供……使用,为……所用”。</strong></font>
    
    - **regular :**
    
      **adj.定时的，定期的;固定的;正常的;均匀的;有规律的，**
      **n.常客，正式成员，固定成员，正式职工;**
      **adv.按时地，定期地;经常;完全;非常**
    
    - **regularly**
    
      **adv.有规律地;经常;间隙均匀地;均匀地;匀称地**





## lesson 44

1. The heavy storm<u><font color=red><strong>      dying down    </strong></font></u>at last, everyone on the island felt released.(die)

   狂风暴雨最后**渐渐平息**了,岛上的每个人都松了一口气。

   <font color=red><strong>dying down</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>die down“渐渐平息,渐渐消失”;前后两分句的主语不一致,且没有连接词连接,故用独立主格结构;the heavy storm与 die down之间为逻辑上的主动关系,故用动词-ing形式。</strong></font>

   1. **"At last" 表示最终、终于，强调经历了漫长的等待或困难后终于实现了某事。**

      **We waited for hours for the rain to stop, and at last it cleared up(我们等了好几个小时雨才停下来，最后雨放晴了)**

   2. **Finally：表示最后，终于的意思，常用于描述一件经历漫长等待之后的结果。**

      **Finally, the long-awaited book has been published.**

   3. **Eventually：意为“最终”，“终于”，表示经过一段时间或经历后最终发生的事情。**

      **Eventually, I found the key that I had lost.**

   4. **In the end：意为“最后”，“终究”，表示经历一番波折或经过一段时间的思考后得出的结论或结果。**

      **In the end, I decided to quit my job and pursue my dream.**

   5. **At length：意为“终于”，“最终”，表示经过一段时间或一番波折后最终得到的结果或结论。**

      **At length, the company announced its decision to merge with another firm.**

   6. **Ultimately：意为“最终”，“终究”，表示在经历了一些变化或困难后最终取得的成果或结果。**

      **Ultimately, the team won the championship after a long and hard-fought season.**

   7. **released  作为动词的过去分词，通常表示释放、发行、发布等意思；而作为形容词时，通常表示被释放的、解脱的、放松的等意思。**

   8. **released v.释放;放出;放走;放开;松开;使自由移动(或飞翔、降落等);发泄;**

2. My demand is that the information referred to in my report<u><font color=red><strong>     (should) be sent to          </strong></font></u>Mr Brown without any delay. (send)

   我的要求是,我的报告中提及的信息**要**及时**传送给**布朗先生。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) be sent to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>demand“要求”,之后的表语从句中用虚拟语气,即从句的谓语动词用“should+动词原形”,should可省略;send.. . to sb.“把……传送给某人”,此处send与the information 之间为动宾关系,故用被动语态；"referred to in my report"是过去分词作定语，用于修饰 "the information"，表达被动的意思，即“在我报告中提到的信息”。</strong></font>

   1. **command：命令，要求，控制**
   2. **mandate：授权，命令，要求**
   3. **request：请求，要求**
   4. **require：要求，需要**
   5. **claim：索要，要求**
   6. **solicit：请求，恳求**
   7. **entreat：请求，乞求**

   这些单词都有表示“要求，请求，控制”等意义，但在不同的语境中可能会有细微的区别。

3. Our school, which<u><font color=red><strong>    was set up         </strong></font></u>in 1945，lies in the south of Changchun City. (set)

   我们学校**建于**1945年,位于长春市的南部。

   <font color=red><strong>was set up</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>set up“建立”,与our school之间为动宾关系,故用被动语态,且由时间状语in 1945可知用一般过去时。</strong></font>

   1. **Set up: 建立、设立 例如: We need to set up a meeting to discuss the new project. (我们需要设立一次会议来讨论新项目。)**
   2. **Set off: 出发、启程 例如: We set off early in the morning to avoid traffic. (我们一早出发以避开交通拥堵。)**
   3. **Settle down: 安定下来、定居 例如: After years of traveling, she finally settled down in a small town. (多年的旅行之后，她最终在一个小镇安定下来。)**
   4. **Set aside: 留出、拨出 例如: He always sets aside time for exercise every day. (他每天都会留出时间进行锻炼。)**
   5. **Set out: 开始、出发、列举 例如: She set out to write a novel last year. (去年她开始写小说。) / The report sets out the details of the investigation. (这份报告列举了调查的详细内容。)**
   6. **Set back: 推迟、延误 例如: The bad weather has set back our construction schedule. (恶劣的天气延误了我们的建设进度。)**
   7. **Set in: 开始、到来 例如: The cold weather has set in early this year. (今年寒冷天气来得早。)**
   8. **Settle up: 结清、付清账款 例如: I need to settle up with the landlord before moving out. (我需要在搬出前结清与房东的账款。)**

4. The more careful you are in the exam,<u><font color=red><strong>       the fewer mistakes        </strong></font></u>you will make. (mistake)

   考试中你越细心，你犯的**错误就越少**。

   <font color=red><strong>the fewer mistakes</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由前半句中的the more和“越”可知,该句用了“the十比较级...,the+比较级...”结构;mistake为可数名词,故用 few修饰具复效形式，具比较级为fewer。</strong></font>

5. The man has been out of work for almost four years. He<u><font color=red><strong>     must have experienced      </strong></font></u>a lot of difficulties. (experience)

   这个人已经失业将近四年了。他**一定经历了**很多困难。

   <font color=red><strong>must have experienced</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去清况的肯定的推测用must have done的形式。</strong></font>

   - **difficulty : n.困难;难题;难事;**

   - **difficult ：adj.困难的;费力的;**

   - **different ：adj.不同的;有区别的;有差异的;分别的;**

     It's different now than it was a year ago.

   - **differently ：adv.不同地；相异地**

     Every individual learns differently...（每个人的学习方式都不一样。）

   - **difference ：n.差别;差异;不同(之处);**

     What's the difference between high school and college?（高中和大学之间有什么不同？）

6. Danny left word with my secretary<u><font color=red><strong>     that he would leave       </strong></font></u>in the afternoon. (leave)

   丹尼给我的秘书留言说下午**他就离开**。

   <font color=red><strong>that he would leave</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>that 引导同位语从句,用来解释说明word的内容,that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略; leave表示的动作是从过去某个时间看来将要发生的,故用过去将来时。</strong></font>

   **leave sth with sb : 把某物交给某人**

7. The play may be several hours late, in which case<u><font color=red><strong>     there is no point（in） waiting      </strong></font></u>.(point)

   这部戏可能要晚几个小时，那样的话**等着就没有意义了**。

   <font color=red><strong>there is no point（in） waiting</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>There is/was no point in doing sth.“做某事没有意义”,其中in可省略。</strong></font>

   **in which case 在那种情况下;那样的话;在那种情况下**

8. Do you know <u><font color=red><strong>     where I can find    </strong></font></u> a second-hand carpet cleaner? （find)

   你知道**我在哪里可以找到**一个二手的地毯吸尘器吗?

   <font color=red><strong>where I can find</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>where引导宾语从句,开在从句中作地点状语,宾语从句中用陈述语序。</strong></font>

9. Mother always tells me that<u><font color=red><strong>     helping others      </strong></font></u>is the source of happiness. (help)

   妈妈总是告诉我,**帮助别人**是快乐的源泉。

   <font color=red><strong>helping others</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导的宾语从句中缺少主语,应用动词-ing形式的短语作从句主语,表示某种概念或经验。</strong></font>

   - **happiness : n.幸福;愉快;(用语等的)适当;幸运**
   - **kindness ：n.仁慈;善良;体贴;宽容;友好的举动**
   - **source ：n.来源;出处;信息来源;原始资料;**
   - **resource ：n.资源;财力;有助于实现目标的东西;资料;勇气;才智;谋略**
     **vt.向…提供资金(或设备)**

10. The teacher and the students<u><font color=red><strong>    were visiting       </strong></font></u>the museum when the earthquake struck. (visit)

    地震发生时，老师和学生们**正在参观**博物馆。

    <font color=red><strong>were visiting</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

    <font color=red><strong>表示过去某个时间正在进行的动作用过去进行时,且主语为 the teacher and the students,故谓语动词用复数形式。</strong></font>
    
    **【不规则形式】 strike struck, struck**





## lesson 45

1. The commander gave the order that all the soldiers<u><font color=red><strong>      should stay where they were        </strong></font></u>that night. (stay)

   指挥官下命令说，所有的士兵当晚都**应该待在他们所在的地方**。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) stay where they were</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>order“命令”,其后的同位语从句中用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should+动词原形”,should可省略;stay后的宾语从句中引导词在句中作地点状语,故用 where。</strong></font>

2. Do you know the singer and dancer who<u><font color=red><strong>    is standing at the gate       </strong></font></u>?(stand)

   你认识**正站在门口**的那个歌唱家兼舞蹈家吗?

   <font color=red><strong>is standing at the gate</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>the singer and dancer指兼有歌唱家和舞蹈家两个身份的同一个人,故谓语动词用单数形式;表示“在门口”应用介词at;由句意可知用现在进行时。</strong></font>

3. I know I was a naive fool to trust him, but he is a real charmer who totally<u><font color=red><strong>        took me in          </strong></font></u>.(take)

   我知道我是个天真的傻瓜，竟然相信他但是他真的是一个善于施展魅力的人，**让我**完全**受骗了**。

   <font color=red><strong>took me in</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由“I was a naive fool to trust him”可知,“他欺骗我”是发生在过去的事情,故用一般过去时; take in“欺骗”。</strong></font>

   **totally : adv.完全地;完全;全部地;整个地**

4. Not<u><font color=red><strong>      knowing her address           </strong></font></u>，I might as well telephone her to come over. (know)

   我不**知道她的地址**，我还不如打电话让她过来。

   <font color=red><strong>knowing her address</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>现在分词短语"Not knowing her address"，它作为原因状语，表明我不知道她的地址是为什么我需要打电话给她；将分词短语"Not knowing her address"改写成普通句子时，需要加上主语和谓语动词，同时将分词短语转化为一个从句，可以改写为："Because I don't know her address, I might as well telephone her to come over." 或者 "As I don't know her address, I might as well telephone her to come over." 这两个句子的意思是一样的，只是表达方式略有不同。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>I 与not know之间为逻辑上的主动关系,故用动词-ing形式作状语,表示原因。</strong></font>

   - **might as well  只好(做);(做…)也无妨;(几乎)和…一样**

     If no one else wants it, we might as well give it to him. （如果没人要这个，我们不妨给他吧。）

   -  **come over  过来;抓住;发生;**

   - **"As well"是一个常用的短语，在英语中有多种用法：**

     1. **"As well" 可以表示“也、同样”。例如：“She speaks Spanish as well as French.”（她不仅会说法语，也会说西班牙语。）**
     2. **"As well" 也可以表示“也要、也可以”。例如：“I'll have a coffee as well.”（我也要一杯咖啡。）**
     3. **"As well" 还可以表示“此外、另外、还有”。例如：“We need eggs, milk, and bread. Oh, and butter as well.”（我们需要鸡蛋、牛奶和面包。哦，还有黄油。）**
     4. **"As well" 还可以表示“同样地、也一样”。例如：“He's always working hard and expects others to do the same as well.”（他总是很努力工作，也期待别人也一样。）**

5. They sometimes<u><font color=red><strong>      found it is difficult/hard to concentrate        </strong></font></u>when reading, but fortunately, their teacher helped them out at last. (concentrate)

   有时候他们**发现**阅读时**集中注意力很困难**，但幸运的是，他们的老师最终帮助他们解决了问题。

   <font color=red><strong>found it is difficult/hard to concentrate</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式宾语，真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

   **help sb out ：帮助某人;帮助某人解决难题，帮助某人摆脱困境，帮助某人完成工作**

6. It was still uncertain<u><font color=red><strong>        whether he would go along           </strong></font></u>with us to visit our teacher. (go)

   还不确定**他是否会**和我们**一起去**探望我们的老师。

   <font color=red><strong>whether he would go along</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的从句,whether引导主语从句,意为“是否”"；因为主句中使用的是过去时态的"was"，所以从句中要使用相应的过去时态来保持时态的一致，即"whether he would go"。</strong></font>

   <strong>"go along with"是一个英语短语，表示同意或支持某人或某事物，也可以表示跟随或一起前往某处。可以用中文翻译为“支持，赞同”或“跟随，一起前往”。例如：</strong>

   - <strong>I will go along with your plan.（我会支持你的计划。）</strong>
   - <strong>She decided to go along with her friends to the party.（她决定和她的朋友一起去参加聚会。）</strong>

7. It is the protection of trees<u><font color=red><strong>      that matters         </strong></font></u>,rather than how many trees are planted. (matter)

   **重要的**是保护树木而非种了多少树木。

   <font color=red><strong>that matters</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>该句中用到了强调句式“It+be十被强调部分＋that...”,被强调部分为“the protection of trees”,其中 that不能省略。</strong></font>

8. Their performance includes rhythm and rhyming words as well as tongue twister, which<u><font color=red><strong>    makes the audience applaud       </strong></font></u>.(make)

   他们的表演包括节奏、韵律以及绕口令,这些使他们经常**赢得观众的掌声**。

   <font color=red><strong>makes the audience applaud</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>make后跟不带to的不定式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

9. One should stick to<u><font color=red><strong>   whatever he has begun/started    </strong></font></u>no matter how difficult it is. (whatever)

   一个人应该坚持**他已经开始的任何事情**,不管有多么困难。

   <font color=red><strong>whatever he has begun/started</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>whatever引导宾语从句,开在从句中作宾语。</strong></font>

   **"Stick to"是一个短语动词，意为“坚持；遵守；忠于”。例如：**

   - **You should stick to your goals if you want to succeed.（如果你想成功，你应该坚持自己的目标。）**
   - **He always sticks to his principles, no matter what.（无论发生什么，他总是遵守自己的原则。）**
   - **I'll stick to the plan we agreed on.（我会遵守我们达成的计划。）**

   **常见的搭配有：**

   - **stick to + 名词：坚持做某事、遵守规定、保持信念等；**
   - **stick to + 动词原形：坚持某种习惯或做法、坚持自己的决定等；**
   - **stick to + 代词/名词/动词-ing：坚持某个方向、坚持自己的观点、坚持自己的工作等。**

10. No sooner had I entered the classroom<u><font color=red><strong>       than the bell rang      </strong></font></u>.(ring)

    我刚一-进入教室,**铃就响了**。
    
    <font color=red><strong>than the bell rang</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>no sooner.. . than.. .“—……就…·引导时间状语从句。</strong></font>





## lesson 46

1. Although that lady is very young, she has two children, who are<u><font color=red><strong>      of the same age      </strong></font></u>.(of)

   尽管那位女士非常年轻,但是她已经有两个孩子了,**他们的年龄一样**。

   <font color=red><strong>of an age/of the same age</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示“年龄相同”应用be of an age或be of the same age.</strong></font>

   **She learned to swim at the age of five.**

   **她在五岁时学会了游泳**

2. We regret<u><font color=red><strong>     to inform you       </strong></font></u>that we have no positions available for someone of your excellent qualifications. (inform)

   我们很遗憾地**通知您**，我们没有适合您这种有杰出资历的人的职位。

   <font color=red><strong>to inform you</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>regret后跟不定式表示对将要做的事情感到遗憾。</strong></font>

   - **position**

     **n.位置;地方;恰当位置;正确位置;vt.安装;安置;使处于**

   - **excellent** 

     **adj.杰出的;极好的;非凡的;**

   - **qualification**

     **n.(通过经验或具备技能而取得的)资格;资历;学历;限定条件;获得资格**

3. I'm afraid you cannot listen to the weather report now. The radio I<u><font color=red><strong>       had repaired         </strong></font></u>yesterday is broken again today. (repair)

   恐怕你现在不能听天气预报。昨天我**让人修**的收音机今天又坏了。

   <font color=red><strong>had repaired</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>have后可跟动词-ed形式作宾语补足语,表示the radio是repair这一列作的承受者;结合时间状语yesterday可知用一般过去时；have sth. done“使某物被做”</strong></font>

4. The young coach must have thought Johnson was worth it, or she<u><font color=red><strong>      wouldn't have wasted        </strong></font></u>so much time on him. (waste)

   年轻的教练一定认为约翰逊值得这样，否则她**不会**在他身上**浪费**那么多时间。

   <font color=red><strong>couldn't/wouldn't nave wasted</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>由语境及关键词or可知,此处是对过去情沉的否定虚拟,此时主句谓语动词用couldn't/wouldn't have done的形式。</strong></font>

   be worth to：值得做

5. <u><font color=red><strong>   It is a matter of time         </strong></font></u>before they will discover that John has left. (matter)

   他们会发现约翰已经离开了,**这只是个时间问题**。

   <font color=red><strong>It is a matter of time</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>it在句中作形式主语,真正的主语是后面的从句。</strong></font>

6. Guess <u><font color=red><strong>    whom I came across           </strong></font></u>in the town yesterday! My primary school maths teacher! (come)

   猜猜我昨天在镇上**碰到了谁**!我的小学数学老师!

   <font color=red><strong>who/whom I came across</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>who/whom引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语,不能省略;come across“偶遇,碰到”。</strong></font>

   **Guess：**

   - **vt. 猜测；认为；推测；猜中**
   - **vi. 猜；推测；猜中**
   - **n. 猜测；推测**

7. He lost his job and meanwhile, the house was too expensive, so he couldn't afford<u><font color=red><strong>       to buy it         </strong></font></u>.(buy)

   他失业了，同时房子也太贵了,因此他**买不起**。

   <font color=red><strong>to buy it</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>afford后跟不定式作宾语。</strong></font>

   **meanwhile**

   - **adv. 与此同时；在此期间；另一方面**
   - **n. 其间，其时**

   **afford to do :有经济条件做某事，负担得起做**

8. Sometimes cells either divide too fast or at the wrong time,<u><font color=red><strong>        which makes it difficult        </strong></font></u>for the body to function properly. (make)

   有时细胞要么分裂得太快要么分裂得不是时候,**这使**身体难以准确地运行。

   <font color=red><strong>which makes it difficult</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>which引导非限制性定语从句,引导词指前面整个分句提到的事实,并在从句中作主语,故谓语动词用单数形式;it在从句中作形式宾语,真正的宾语是后面的不定式短语。</strong></font>

   1. **properly：*adv.*正确地，适当地；得体地，恰当地；实际上，严格地说；彻底地**

   2. **function ：**

      - **n. 功能，职责；宴会，典礼；函数，应变量；由其他事情造成的结果；子例行程序，子例程；官能团，功能团**
      - **v. 工作，运转；行使职责，发挥功能**

   3. **"Either", "neither", 和 "nor" 都是用于表示否定选择或否定关系的词语，它们在句子中起到连接的作用。**

      1. **"Either" （或者）用于表示在两个选择之间的肯定关系。它通常与 "or" 连用，用于在肯定的选择之间做出选择。**

         **例如：**

         1. **You can either have tea or coffee. （你可以喝茶或咖啡。）**
         2. **Either John or Mary will pick you up from the airport. （要么是约翰，要么是玛丽会去机场接你。）**

      2. **"Neither" （也不）用于表示否定的选择关系。它通常与 "nor" 连用，用于否定的选择之间。**

         **例如：**

         1. **Neither Tom nor Sarah could attend the meeting. （汤姆和莎拉都不能参加会议。）**
         2. **I have neither the time nor the resources to complete the project. （我既没有时间也没有资源完成这个项目。）**

      3. **"Nor" （也不）用于否定句中，连接两个否定要素。它常与 "neither" 连用，形成否定选择关系。**

         **例如：**

         1. **I don't like coffee, nor do I like tea. （我不喜欢咖啡，也不喜欢茶。）**
         2. **He didn't study for the test, nor did he ask for help. （他没有为考试学习，也没有寻求帮助。）**

      **总结起来，"either" 表示肯定选择关系，"neither" 表示否定选择关系，而 "nor" 用于否定句中连接两个否定要素。**

9. The news<u><font color=red><strong>          that the plane would take off        </strong></font></u>on time made everyone at the airport happy. (take)

   **飞机将**按时**起飞**的消息让机场里的每个人都很高兴。

   <font color=red><strong>that the plane would take off</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>that引导同位语从句,用来解释说明news的内容, that在从句中不作任何成分,也无实际意义,只起连接作用,不能省略;take off“起飞”。</strong></font>

10. The film<u><font color=red><strong>      might have ended        </strong></font></u>by now, because the crowd are flooding out of the cinema (end)

    现在电影**大概已经结束了**，因为人群正从电影院里涌出来。
    
    <font color=red><strong>may/might have ended</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>表示“大概”应用情态动词may或might;此处表示对过去情况的推测,其后接have done的形式。</strong></font>
    





## lesson 47

1. She<u><font color=red><strong>        must have had          </strong></font></u>a very hard time, for her good friend couldn't recognize her when they met in a park years later. (have)

   她**一定度过了**一段非常艰难的时光，因为多年以后她的好朋友和她在公园里相遇时认不出她了。

   <font color=red><strong>must have had</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>表示对过去情况的肯定推测用 must have done的形式。</strong></font>

2. As a nurse,<u><font color=red><strong>      what she wants to do       </strong></font></u>is to look after the orphans coming from that poor mountain area.(what)

   作为护士，**她想要做的**就是照顾那些来自那个贫穷山区的孤儿们。

   <font color=red><strong>what she wants to do</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>what引导主语从,并在从句中作宾语；现在分词短语coming from作定语</strong></font>

   **orphan**

   - **n. 孤儿**
   - **v. 成为孤儿**

3. Rich countries have a responsibility towards poor countries and must do<u><font color=red><strong>       all what they can          </strong></font></u>to help others. (can)

   富裕的国家对贫穷的国家有责任,并且必须尽**他们所能**去帮助他人。

   <font color=red><strong>all(that)/what they can</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>what 引导宾语从句,并在从句中作宾语,相当于 all that,其中 that 可省略。</strong></font>

   - **have a responsibility towards ：对…有责任**
   - **be responsible for :对……负责；是……的原因**

4. As time went by, the new idiom <u><font color=red><strong>     came into being      </strong></font></u>and was widely used later. (come)

   随着时间的流逝，这个新习语**产生了,**并且接着就被广泛使用。

   <font color=red><strong>came into being</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>come into being“产生出现”,由句中时态可知用般过去时。</strong></font>

   - **as time go by：随着时间的推移**

     **As time go by my memory seem to get worse.** 

     **随著时间的流逝，我的记忆力似乎越来越差。**

   - **idiom**

     **n. 习语，成语；方言，土话；（个人、艺术形式等的）风格，特色**

   - **idiot**

     **n. 白痴，笨蛋；<古>弱智者，低能儿**

5. Whenever he was asked why he was late for class, he would answer carelessly, always<u><font color=red><strong>    saying the same excuse         </strong></font></u>.(say)

   不管什么时候问他为什么上课迟到,他都心不在焉地回答，总是**说同样的借口**。

   <font color=red><strong>saying the same excuse</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>he 与 say 之间为逻辑上的主动关系，故用动词-ing形式作伴随状语。</strong></font>

6. <u><font color=red><strong>        How do you respond to        </strong></font></u>someone who proposes constructing the world's tallest building? (respond)

   **你如何回应**建议建造世界最高建筑的人?

   <font color=red><strong>How do you respond to</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>此为 how 引导的特殊疑问句；respond后跟宾语时，宾语前应加介词 to。</strong></font>

   1. **propose ：提议做某事**

      **What do you propose doing next?**

   2. **purpose**

      ***n.*目的，意图；目标，计划；（达到生活中目标的）决心**

      ***v.*有意，打算**

   3. **construct**

      ***v.*建造，修建；组成，创立，构思；绘制，作图**

      ***n.*构想，观念；**

7. When the poor man came to life, he found himself<u><font color=red><strong>     tied to a tree        </strong></font></u>.(tie)

   当这个穷人醒过来的时候,他发现自己**被绑在一棵树上**。

   <font color=red><strong>tied to a tree</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>find 后可跟动词-ed 形式作宾语补足语，表被动和完成，表示himself是tie 这一动作的承受者;tie...to...“把··...·绑在.....上”。</strong></font>

8. He <u><font color=red><strong>       who has passed      </strong></font></u>the exam will be given the driving license. (pass)

   **已经通过**考试的人将会得到驾照。

   <font color=red><strong>who has passed</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>who引导定语从句,并在从句中作主语,由句意及句子结构可知用现在完成时。</strong></font>

9. How I wish I<u><font color=red><strong>        hadn't tried        </strong></font></u>to repair the watch! I only made it worse. (try)

   我多么希望自己**没有尽力**去修这块表!我只是把它搞得更糟了。

   <font color=red><strong>hadn't tried</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>wish 后跟宾语从句时,从句用虚拟语气，且此处表示与过去事实相反,故谓语动词用过去完成时。</strong></font>

10. When driving on the mountain area, we saw signs everywhere warning people<u><font color=red><strong>     to look out for        </strong></font></u>falling rocks. (look)

    当在山区驾驶的时候，我们看到到处都是提醒人们**当心**落石的警示语。
    
    <font color=red><strong>to look out for</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>解析：</strong></font>
    
    <font color=red><strong>warn 后跟不定式作宾语补足语;look out for“当心,小心”</strong></font>
    
    1. **warn sb not to do**
    
       **警告不要做**
    
    2. **warn sb to do**
    
       **提醒某人去做某事**





##  lesson 48

1. About 10% of the people on the earth now<u><font color=red><strong>      don't have access to       </strong></font></u>clean drinking water. (access)

   地球上大约10%的人现在**不能喝到**干净的饮用水。

   <font color=red><strong>don't have access to/have no access to</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>“百分数+名词”作主语时,谓语动词的单复数由该名词决定,故此处用复数形式; </strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>have access to“可接近,可以达到,可以使用”,此处用否定形式,可借助助动词do和可直接用no access.</strong></font>

2. I can't read the advertisement on the board. Could you hold the light<u><font color=red><strong>      closer to it          </strong></font></u>? (close)

   我看不到公告板上的广告。你能把灯拿得**离它近一点**吗?

   <font color=red><strong>closer to it</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>close的副词形式仍为close,其比较级形式为closer; close应与介词to搭配。</strong></font>

   **abroad：国外**

3. <u><font color=red><strong>        The first time I saw            </strong></font></u><u><font color=red><strong>  </strong></font></u>her, I thought she was very gentle and kind-hearted. (time)

   **我第一次**看见她时，我以为她非常温柔善良。

   <font color=red><strong>The first time I saw</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>名词短语the first time可用来引导时间状语从句,表示“第一次……的时候”</strong></font>

   - **gentle ：adj. 文静的，温柔的；v. 使（或变）温柔**

   - polite：有礼貌的，客气的；礼节性的，客套的；上流的，有教养的；

   - courteous：有礼貌的，谦恭的；

   - **hearted ：**

     **adj. 呈……心情的；有……之心的；放在心上的**

     **v. 铭记；用心材支撑；结心（heart 的过去分词）**

4. I happened<u><font color=red><strong>        to have talked with         </strong></font></u>the man interviewing me before I came here. (talk)

   我在来这里之前刚好**和**面试我的人**说过话**。

   <font color=red><strong>to have talked with </strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>happen后跟不定式作宾语;由“说过话”或者before I came here可知,应用完成时;talk with“与……谈话”。</strong></font>

5. Are you really reading the newspaper? You<u><font color=red><strong>     are holding it upside down         </strong></font></u>,So don't cheat me any more. (hold)

   你真的在读这张报纸吗?你**把它拿倒了**，所以不要再骗我了。

   <font color=red><strong>are holding it upside down</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>表示现在正在进行的动作用现在进行时;upside down“上下颠倒”。</strong></font>

6. So fast<u><font color=red><strong>       did he run         </strong></font></u>that I couldn't catch up with him though I was already out of breath. (run)

   **他跑得**如此快以至于我追不上他,尽管我已经上气不接下气了

   <font color=red><strong>did he run</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>so...that...结构中的so修饰的副词置于句首时主句应用部分倒装。</strong></font>

7. I suggested that he<u><font color=red><strong>      (should) adapt to             </strong></font></u>the new condition as soon as possible, or it would be difficult for him to carry on.(adapt)

   我建议他尽快**适应**新环境，否则他将很难继续下去。

   <font color=red><strong>(should) adapt to </strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>suggest意为“建议”时,其后的宾语从句中用虚拟语气,谓语动词用“should＋动词原形”,should可省略;adapt to“适应”。</strong></font>

   **as soon as possible ：尽快 /尽可能快 /越快越好 /尽可能**

8. <u><font color=red><strong>        why that photo became        </strong></font></u>his greatest glory was a very interesting story. (become)

   **为什么那张照片成了**他最大的荣耀是一个非常有趣的故事。

   <font color=red><strong>Why that photo/picture became</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>why 引导主语从句,并在从句中作原因状语。</strong></font>

9. They keep<u><font color=red><strong>        asking me to join       </strong></font></u>their social club but I prefer to go my own way. (ask)

   他们一直**让我加人**他们的社交俱乐部,但是我更愿意走自己的路。

   <font color=red><strong>asking me to join</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>keep后跟动词-ing形式作宾语;ask后跟不定式作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

   <font color=red><strong>"keep doing"：表示持续进行某种行为，指继续做之前已经在进行的动作。这个结构中，动词以现在分词形式（-ing 形式）出现。</strong></font>

10. The two things in<u><font color=red><strong>       which they take pride         </strong></font></u>are Jim's watch and Lucy's hair.(pride)

    **他们引以为豪**的两件东西是吉姆的表和露西的头发。
    
    <font color=red><strong>which they take pride</strong></font>
    
    **解析：**
    
    <font color=red><strong>take pride in“以……为自豪”;该短语中的介词in提至从句句首,且先行词指物,故只能用which引导定语从句。</strong></font>
    
    **be proud of：为..感到骄傲，以...自豪**





##  lesson 49

1. The problem is<u><font color=red><strong>     far from being        </strong></font></u>solved, so it has to be discussed again.(far)

   问题**远没有**解决，因此还得再讨论一次

   <font color=red><strong>far from being</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>far from“远离”;介词from后应跟动词-ing形式。</strong></font>

   **"Far from" 是一个常用的短语，表示距离或程度上的远离，也可用来表示与预期或期望相反。以下是它的几种常见用法：**

   1. **表示距离：指两个地点或物体之间的远离。**
      - **The hotel is far from the airport.（酒店离机场很远。）**
      - **The grocery store is far from our house.（杂货店离我们家很远。）**

   2. **表示程度：表示某事物超出了一定程度，表达程度上的强调。**
      - **He is far from happy about the situation.（他对这种情况远非满意。）**
      - **The performance was far from perfect.（这次表演远非完美。）**

   3. **表示与预期或期望相反：表示某事与人们的预期或期望相反。**
      - **The result was far from what I expected.（结果与我预期的迥然不同。）**
      - **The movie was far from being entertaining.（这部电影远非有趣。）**
   4. **远非做某事：表示某人没有或不愿意做某事。**
      - **He is far from being helpful.（他远非乐于助人。）**
      - **The company is far from meeting its sales targets.（该公司远未达到销售目标。）**
   5. **远非达到某种状态或水平：表示未达到预期的状态或水平。**
      - **The project is far from completion.（这个项目远未完成。）**
      - **Her performance is far from satisfactory.（她的表现远未令人满意。）**
   6. **远非具备某种特征或品质：表示与某种特征或品质相反或迥异。**
      - **The situation is far from ideal.（这种情况远非理想。）**
      - **The product is far from perfect.（这个产品远非完美。）**

   **需要注意的是，"far from" 通常与动词、形容词、副词等修饰词连用，用来描述距离或程度上的远离。**

2. Only by changing the way we live<u><font color=red><strong>     can we save      </strong></font></u>the earth. (save)

   只有通过改变我们的生活方式，**我们才能拯救**地球。

   <font color=red><strong>can we save</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>only强调状语置于句首时句子用部分倒装,根据句意,助动词用can。</strong></font>

3. Water, which seems so simple and common, is<u><font color=red><strong>          what makes life possible        </strong></font></u>.(what)

   水看似如此简单、普通，却是**使生命成为可能的东西。**

   <font color=red><strong>what makes life possible</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>what 引导表语从句,并在从句中作主语;make后可跟形容词作宾语补足语。</strong></font>

4. If<u><font color=red><strong>          I were you          </strong></font></u>,I would never say such kind of words to my younger brother or sister. (be)

   如果**我是你**，我永远不会对我的弟弟或妹妹说这样的话。

   <font color=red><strong>I were you</strong></font>

   **解析：**

   <font color=red><strong>if引导的非真实条件句中,表示与现在事实相反的虚拟语气时,作从句谓语的be动词应用 were.</strong></font>

5. The development of technology has<u><font color=red><strong>       made it possible      </strong></font></u>for us to get in touch with each other more easily. (make)

   科技的发展**使**我们更加容易地联系彼此**成为可能**。
